minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郭永凤</span><b 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭元荣、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">果然、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">果•喜饶嘉措（藏）</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">岗吉•志巴加（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1981</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日出生，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Gangkye Drubpa Kyab</span>（</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;Microsoft Himalaya&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">གངས་སྐྱེས་སྒྲུབ་པ་སྐྱབས།</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">），又被译为岗吉珠巴嘉，四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治州（简称甘孜州）色达县人，原色达县霍西乡某私立学校教师，笔名血火狮（藏语称“岗麦达”），藏族知名作家，政治异见人士，中国在押政治犯。作为作家，曾用藏文撰写并出版《命运的呼喊（</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;Microsoft Himalaya&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">ལས་དབང་གི་རྒྱང་འབོད</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">）》、《时代的悲痛（</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;Microsoft Himalaya&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">དུས་ཀྱི་ན་ཟུག</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">）》、《今日的眼泪（</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;Microsoft Himalaya&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">དེ་རིང་གི་མིག་ཆུ</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">）》、《<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年全境红色血书（</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;Microsoft Himalaya&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">༢༠༠༨ལོའི་ས་བྱི་ཁྲག་བྲིས་དམར་པོ་</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">）》等多部著作，涉猎小说、杂文、评述、诗歌等多种文体，并曾独立编辑两份藏文报刊《岁月的颜色》（</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;Microsoft Himalaya&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">ལོ་ཟླའི་ཁ་དོག</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">）与《洁白哈达》（</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;Microsoft Himalaya&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">ཁ་བཏགས་དཀར་པོའི་ཚགས་དེབ</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">），故而获得藏区同胞读者的广泛好评；虽然其多数作品并无明显触及中共当局敏感神经的话题，仅表达了其对藏族文化、藏族宗教信仰以及对民族和故乡故土的深厚情感，但因其两首短诗揭露了<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年中共镇压西藏期间，藏民遭受的痛苦折磨以及在铺天盖地的官员贪腐和牟取暴利之下，百姓所面临的艰难处境，遂很快引起发了中共四川当局的高度紧张，并成为被政府严管监控和伺机打击的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其被甘孜州色达县警方突然莫名抓走，后又被甘孜州雅江县检察院以涉嫌“分裂、危害国家安全罪”正式批捕，指控其因是“西藏活动人士”并建立名为“抗红组织”的团体，遂起言行触犯了国家的法律法规，应予批捕、重判；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，其案在四川省甘孜州法院开庭审理，至同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，终被雅江县法院以“分裂、危害国家安全罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并送色达县监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被减刑提前释放，但次日又因其将达赖喇嘛的法相放在头上而被当局指其认罪“态度不良”，故又被色达县派出所警方拘留<span lang="EN-US">17</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，其再次因之前撰写并发表过数本有关西藏命运及局势的书本和报刊，并且创建了“反红抵抗组织”，而被甘孜州色达县警方以涉嫌“分裂和危害国家安全罪”拘捕；与其同期被捕的另有<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名同区域藏人作家及社会活动人士，涉嫌罪名相同；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，其一行<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人案在四川省甘孜州中级法院开庭审理，最终被以“分裂、危害国家安全罪”统一判处<span lang="EN-US">4-14</span>年不等刑期；其中，其被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2035</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日；据悉，首次服刑期间，曾惨遭狱警酷刑折磨，后因健康持续恶化，狱方才不得不将其提前释放；但获释后，因其身心状况一直未见好转，不仅出现严重的精神障碍，视力及记忆力也急剧下降，肾和胃的功能严重退化，故其现在狱中的身体状况令人堪忧。目前疑似在四川省德阳监狱（四川省德阳市旌阳区黄许镇，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">618007</span>）服刑。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/14_23.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/14_23.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高兵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年生，宁夏法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年修炼法轮功。在<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共开始迫害法轮功时，他是一名高校学生，因不放弃信仰，被开除。因不放弃修炼，此前他曾被判刑两次均为<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并被拘禁在洗脑班近<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。共曾遭牢狱迫害<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日高兵又遭盐池县花马池警察抓捕，下落不明。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月获悉，<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">高兵已遭判刑，被关押在宁夏石嘴山监狱</span>。此次高兵<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">被判刑的时间及刑期、关押到监狱的时间等情况均不详</span>。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高崇文：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New lang="EN-US">50</span>岁左右，以送快递为生，家有<span lang="EN-US">70</span>多岁老母亲。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，高崇文讲法轮功，被警察抓捕，家用电脑等私人物品被抄。后来高崇文被检察院批捕，被关押在凌源看守所。后获悉其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。高崇文现在被关押在沈阳监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">高方强：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">男，<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">山东泰安市法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年年五十二岁，个体业主。<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">2020</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日上午，谢清玲、高方强等法轮功学员去良庄镇赠送法轮功年历，在回来的路上，警察驾驶围堵抓捕。后泰山区公安分局国保大队与岱庙等派出所撬门破锁，闯入谢清玲家中，将家中所有电脑、打印机、法轮功资料等物品抄走。谢清玲和高方强最后被关押到泰安市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月获悉谢清玲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，罚款两万元；高方强被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。谢清玲和高方强不服，上诉至泰安市中级法院。泰安中院裁定“维持原判”。后谢清玲转入山东省女子监狱服刑；高方强被转入山东省监狱服刑。高方强刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/2022-1-20.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高国杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京基督徒、企业家。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日北京警方被带走，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被逮捕，涉嫌罪名是“诈骗罪”。高国杰热心公义，多年来在从商的同时参与社会公益事业。北京警方将他与另一位企业家之间的一笔经济往来定为诈骗，现在检察院已经将案件提交到法院，建议量刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>到<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/blog-post_57.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/blog-post_57.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高洪杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省潍坊市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，男，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">原山东省潍坊学院电大教学处教师，山东省安丘市景芝镇口埠村人。<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年他开始修炼法轮功，在中共对法轮功的疯狂迫害中，他坚持信仰，多次被关押，曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月初被山东省安丘市公安局警察抓捕。安丘市法院<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月将他判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并罚金二万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/1/19/455366.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/1/19/455366.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高洪伟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日重庆<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名法轮功学员李嘉惠、张盛全、李玉华、高洪伟、秦雪美被抓捕，两年多后<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月才获悉已经被判刑。高洪伟<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；张盛全、李嘉惠，被枉判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；李玉华<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千元，监外执行；秦雪美<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>千元。高洪伟刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">高华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省葫芦岛市绥中县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日下午，绥中县国保大队副大队长刘唤宇等人，闯到高华家，抓捕了高华和高英姐妹，以及去串门的法轮功学员陈文艳和王彦东，抢劫了高华家的电脑、打印机等私人财物。高华被关押在葫芦岛看守所，高英被关押在葫芦岛拘留所，王彦东被关押在绥中看守所。陈文艳被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，高华、高英、王彦东被构陷到绥中县检察院。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，高英回家，被监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，高华、王彦东被构陷案到了葫芦岛连山检察院，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日高华、王彦东被葫芦岛市连山法院判刑：高华<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，王彦东<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；高华刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/2/%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E8%91%AB%E8%8A%A6%E5%B2%9B%E5%B8%82%E9%AB%98%E5%8D%8E%E3%80%81%E7%8E%8B%E5%BD%A6%E4%B8%9C%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-434280.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/2/%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E8%91%AB%E8%8A%A6%E5%B2%9B%E5%B8%82%E9%AB%98%E5%8D%8E%E3%80%81%E7%8E%8B%E5%BD%A6%E4%B8%9C%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-434280.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高惠仙：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日生，原云南省昆明钢铁公司桥钢厂职工，后被非法开除公职。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共对法轮功持续迫害中，高惠仙曾两次被中共判刑，共遭冤狱九年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日高惠仙向安宁市太平街道办事处龙箐村中共支部书记何顺贵讲法轮功真相，同时赠送了一本「明慧日历」向他祝福。结果何顺贵向公安机关诬告高惠仙。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日高惠仙正在母亲家里，被安宁市国保大队警察非法撬锁入室抓捕、抄家，警察抢走计算机、打印机、大法书籍、法轮功数据等大量私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被昆明市西山区法院判刑七年，罚款一千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高建君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏省连云港市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，连云港市海州区公安分局抓捕了法轮功学员刘玉萍、邵世玲、那仁志、熊成霞、周翠萍、马宝玲、高建君、王艾芝、汪宝玉、小周女士、乔老太等十一人。所有人家中都被非法抄了家，警察劫走家中的电脑、手机、光盘、<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘、电器、钱财、书籍等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，高建君被开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高金平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1947</span>年生，保定市依棉厂退休职工，法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>中午，高金平在保定市满城区出租房内被保定市公安局国保警察和保定市竞秀区依棉派出所抓捕，并同时抢走电脑、大法书籍等个人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，高阳县法院对高金平开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，高金平被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">高菊芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">江西新余市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1958</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，高菊芳到一小区发法轮功资料，被人举报，随后被警察抄家，家里的法像和法轮功书籍全部抄走，被关押到看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月得知，高菊芳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/1/31/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%B8%89%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-419315.html#2113022538-1"><b mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">高俊</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：辽宁省鞍山市人，法轮功信仰者。因信仰、宣传法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日晚在高俊的七岭子家中，高俊、张永宝二人被辽阳公安局警察跟踪绑架、构陷，后经辽阳县法院三次庭审，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日二人被一审以犯“邪教罪”分别冤判有期徒刑。其中，高俊被重判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其不服已提起上诉。张永宝被冤判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高立娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">天津石化公司青年女教师、法轮功学员。高立娟<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被当地警察绑架。高立娟遭构陷的案卷两次被检察院退回，办案单位大港胜利派出所及大港国继续罗列罪名，又把高立娟起诉到天津滨海新区法院，意欲高立娟重判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>到<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年徒刑。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日高立娟案在天津滨海新区法院庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万。高丽娟上诉被驳回。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东淄博市博山区法轮功学员。法轮功学员王忠实、高明洁于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被抓捕、构陷，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被判刑：王忠实获刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，被勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万；高明洁<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，被勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万。二人上诉，被中级法院维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/24/%E6%9B%BE%E9%81%AD%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E6%8A%98%E7%A3%A8-%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E6%B7%84%E5%8D%9A%E5%B8%82%E7%8E%8B%E5%BF%A0%E5%AE%9E%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4-431828.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高鹏 ：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省潍坊市昌乐县五图街道邱家河村法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1987</span>年生。因发放法轮功资料，于<span lang="EN-US"> 2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被抓捕、构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、罚金五万元。依法上诉，潍坊中院维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被关押到山东省监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/1/5/454541.html#231422721-8"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/1/5/454541.html#231422721-8</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高鹏光：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，又名高朋光，黑龙江省牡丹江市穆棱市人，穆棱市八面通镇高峰村公民，法轮功修炼者和信仰者，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代末期起，因其与其姐高永丽二人为强身健体、家庭和睦等而开始锻炼、信仰及宣传法轮功，而屡遭中共黑龙江省穆棱市当局的监控与打压；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，曾因宣传法轮功而被牡丹江市穆棱市国保警方和穆棱市八面通镇第一派出所警方联合非法闯入其家，谎称其邻居丢失手机报案后警方通过手机定位查到其家，故其家强行遭搜查，掠走其大量私人财物及相关法轮功书籍等，现场一片狼藉；后其又被诽谤偷人手机，遂旋即被警方暴力抓捕并被刑拘；看守所羁押期间，因其绝食抗议被非法关押，又遭毒打；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，穆棱市建行小区的法轮功信仰者曹淑芳老人的家中门窗出现破碎，其知晓后，遂与同是法轮功信仰者的孙士伟等人前去帮修，熟料当二人维修完毕准备离开时，却被跟踪赶来的穆棱市警方突然抓捕，同时，警方又将曹淑芳老人本人以及前去慰问、探望的其姐高永丽等人一并抓走；随后，其等<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人各家均被查抄；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，其等<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人又被异地交由牡丹江海林市检察院，以涉嫌“邪教罪”予以批捕，并被关押在穆棱市八面通看守所；后其<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人案被检察院起诉到牡丹江海林市法院；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人案在海林市法院统一开庭受审，期间，其妻和其姐之女被穆棱市警方诱骗到当地派出所签字，就此被视为是其等犯罪的“证人”，并将她们的庭审旁听权取消；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其等<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被海林市法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”统一宣判，其中，其被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US"> 6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；其余<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人亦被分判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月至<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月不等刑期；其等不服，均表提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，经黑龙江省牡丹江市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判；其刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。起初在黑龙江省牡丹江监狱服刑，目前在黑龙江省呼兰监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/66.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/66.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">高伟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山西省太原市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，高伟等太原市八位法轮功学员被警察抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月获悉高伟被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，目前被关押在山西省晋中监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/27/452406.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/27/452406.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%;">高西霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%;">山东省临沂市兰山区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。一九九九年七月江泽民发动对法轮功的迫害之后，高西霞被迫离家在外。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，高西霞到兰山区北园路纽约上城发放真相资料时，被不明真相的人举报，随后被育才路派出所抓捕，第二天她取保候审回到家中。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，派出所和国保以不配合签字为由，在没有搜查证和拘留证的情况下派出所警察及国保人员强行撬她家的门锁，把人带走，并将她家里的银行卡及现金翻走。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，兰山区法院进行了庭审，期间以家属是证人为由，阻止家属旁听，并阻止家属申请亲友辩护，不允许家属为高西霞辩护。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，兰山区法院对高西霞判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://4.31.18.88/mh/articles/2022/3/22/%E4%BC%A0%E6%92%AD%E7%9C%9F%E7%9B%B8-%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E4%B8%B4%E6%B2%82%E5%B8%82%E9%AB%98%E8%A5%BF%E9%9C%9E%E9%81%AD%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-440355.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height:
