style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高贤英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四川泸州市合江县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年七十五岁。高贤英曾被非刑两次，一次<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，一次<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日上午，四川泸州市七名法轮功学员高贤英、董国珍、周明英、张元华、刘忠芬、帅先芳、宋平（男）驱车到泸州市合江县五通镇赶场，被派出所警察抓捕，然后带到合江九支镇派出所审问。后因年纪大，回家监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被四川泸州市合江县法院高显英被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，处罚金七千。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">高晓歧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林农安县法轮功学员。女、<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">56</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，长春市农安县抓捕了<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多名法轮功学员。此次抓捕行动，是由长春市政法委和农安县政法委共同策划实施的。此次被抓捕的法轮功学员有</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张秀芝、高晓歧、蔡玉英、吴冬梅、于姣茹、单为和、赵秀兰、孙秀英、张敬元、孙凤仙、冯立齐、吕相富、董秀辉等<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">22</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">名法轮功学员被抓捕。他们被抓捕、构陷<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，有十几名法轮功学员被德惠市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>至<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。其中：高晓歧被判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，罚金两万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/5/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%9713%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%8C%E5%88%B0%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4-%E4%B8%AD%E6%B3%95%E7%BB%B4%E6%8C%81%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4-434381.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/5/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%9713%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%8C%E5%88%B0%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4-%E4%B8%AD%E6%B3%95%E7%BB%B4%E6%8C%81%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4-434381.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">高永丽</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江穆棱市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日下午，穆棱市建行小区的一位老人曹淑芳家中的玻璃碎了，法轮功学员孙士伟、高朋光、高永丽三人帮其修理。国保警察突然出现抓捕了孙士伟、高朋光、高永丽三人，并抄了三人的家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，海林市法院下判决，高永丽被诬判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，高朋光和孙士伟被诬判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，分别处以两万罚金。高永丽刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/610.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/610.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高智晟：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，陕西省榆林市佳县人，著名维权律师。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年起，开始替弱势群体维权打官司，曾处理过多宗民间维权案件；自<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年底起，开始多次上书中共当局高层，要求改变对法轮功等群体的非法处理手段，并参与对法轮功学员器官遭当局活摘指控的调查；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，与妻子公开宣布退出中国共产党；因其勇于于为当局认定的敏感性案件（注：含法轮功信仰者、地下基督教徒以及与官员发生纠纷的底层农民和私营企业家）辩护，故而曾多次受到中共官方机构或组织（<span lang="EN-US">610</span>办公室）黑社会手段的严重骚扰和打击报复；<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，其执业执照被当局吊销，随后被秘密绑架并遭到约<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月的酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被北京市第一中级法院以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，缓刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日起其与外界失联，至<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月才被当局释放返京；后因其接受了美联社采访，遂被再次与外界失联，直至<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其亲友才从新华社报导中得知，其缓刑已被北京法院撤销，须继续服刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月，至<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日刑满出狱，此前在新疆维吾尔自治区沙雅监狱服刑。出狱后高智晟仍被严密监控，且不让治牙看病，致其因长期在狱中遭受酷刑折磨和被单独囚禁，迄今仍牙齿松动，身体健康欠佳；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其在陕北老家秘密撰写的新书《<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，起来中国》在台湾正式印刷出售，因该书涉及中共当局对其长期绑架、囚禁和施以酷刑等，以及他从信仰角度看中共<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年将会灭亡和对<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年后的中国未来宪政民主化展望等三大内容，遂令当局十分恐惧、恼怒，对其监控愈加严密。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月中旬在老家失踪，后获知被当局控制带回北京关押。目前已遭强迫失踪<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年多，音信全无，生死不明。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">格桑梅朵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">西藏拉萨一小学女教师。格桑梅朵是第一位可以被知道的因翻墙而遭中共当局强迫失踪的藏人。据了解，格桑梅朵曾在<span lang="EN-US">Facebook</span>上转发外媒 《自由亚洲电台》和《挪威西藏之声》中文部有关藏区的新闻报道，以促进使用<span lang="EN-US">Facebook</span>的中国网友，特别是她的汉族朋友们了解西藏问题的真相。梅朵非常了解西藏的历史和现实。格桑梅朵翻墙转发外媒西藏新闻一事被发现后，当局开始对她进行迫害，她所在的小学将梅朵开除，梅朵继而于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年遭到当局强迫失踪，至今已下落不明<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。现获悉，格桑梅朵被以“泄露国家秘密”定罪，关押地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">格桑秀郎（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生不详，西藏那曲地区比如县达木寺僧人。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日在拉萨市被拉萨警方拘捕，后一直被秘密关押，直至<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日获知，其被拉萨市中级法院以“带领民众集会”罪名判处<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年有期徒刑。目前被关押在西藏拉萨的扎其监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">革振华：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">63</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">岁，黑龙江省哈尔滨市阿城区人，原阿城区低压电器厂职工，法轮功学员。因信仰法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年曾被哈尔滨市阿城市公安局非法劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。在哈尔滨市长林子劳教所期间，经常遭到警察和犯人的毒打，被强迫长时间坐小板凳等。因劳教所环境恶劣，他身上长满了疥疮，疼痛难忍。每天还要强迫他做十几个小时的苦役，完不成任务就罚站。其左肋骨曾被警察和犯人打断两根，但仍不放过他，逼他出工干活，一天也不许休息。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日凌晨，他在哈尔滨市尚志市亮河镇挂条幅、散发法轮功宣传资料时，被当地警方闻讯赶来围捕、绑架，后被关押在尚志市看守所。与其一起的法轮功学员菽坤和王翠娥也遭抓捕，至今未归。因长期不知革振华的消息，其妻经多方打听，直至<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月才知道丈夫革振华已被哈尔滨市尚志市法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉法冤判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。据悉，革振华不服，提起上诉，但二审仍维持原判。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。目前服刑地不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">根敦伦珠（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1974</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，青海藏族作家、诗人，曾是青海同仁县隆务寺僧人，过去曾数次被当局逮捕。同仁县熟悉此事的消息人士介绍，根敦伦珠对保护母语藏语文和西藏文化非常关心。他的作品在境内和流亡藏人拥有很大的影响力。根敦伦珠于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年十月在网站上发表了一首诗歌，内容是作家和艺术家需要有言论和思想不受限制的自由。尽管面临诸多限制，根敦伦珠仍坚持创作，并从其读者处获得支持。青海当局制订的藏区“扫黑除恶”政策中，把提倡“保护母语”视为黑恶势力行为。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，青海省黄南州藏族作家、诗人根敦伦珠被中共当局逮捕，关押至秘密地点，下落不明。据悉，当局在对其实施长时间监视后采取了这个行动。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">根托（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川甘孜藏区炉霍县人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，在西藏康区炉霍县境内发生大规模和平示威活动后，中共军警釆取武力镇压，导致云丹为首的多名藏人被开枪打死或打伤，上百人遭捕。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日中共当局对<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名遭捕的藏人进行判决，其中一名藏人被判终身监禁，另有多人遭<span lang="EN-US">1</span>至<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等的有期徒刑。这<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名被判藏人中，已确切得知的有<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名藏人具体情况，其中：根托，现年<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多岁，被判<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">耿福霞<span lang="EN-US">:<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span></span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北唐山市法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日早上<span lang="EN-US">4</span>、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>点钟，唐山丰润区公安局局长刘金良等有计划、有预谋抓捕丰润区法轮功学员耿福霞、王秀红、付瑞英、尉国申、钱淑娟、邱瑞旺、陆彩芸、韩玉芹、肖慧君等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人。<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁的法轮功学员韩玉芹当天被端明路派出所迫害致死。后来，耿福霞、付瑞英、尉国申以不同的病业形式返回家中；王秀红、陆彩芸、钱淑娟、邱瑞旺被转到唐山第一看守所遭受迫害。当时被抓捕的<span lang="EN-US">8</span>名法轮功学员被构陷到遵化市法院。河北唐山市遵化法院<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日对<span lang="EN-US">5</span>位法轮功学员耿福霞、王秀红、尉国申、付瑞英、陆彩云开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日判耿福霞<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">耿家峰：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日出生，山东省沂水县籍人，山东省淄博市桓台县马桥镇辛庄村村民，维权访民，实名举报人，中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年起，就开始因所在村落官员严重贪腐问题而实名举报维权，随被山东省桓台县当局视为需要打压的异己和维稳对象；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，曾因先后三次上访投诉，被恒台县警方以“非正常上访”为由给予严厉警告；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，曾两次被恒台县警方以“非正常上访，扰乱公共场所秩序”为由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，又被以警方“故意损害财物”、“扬言实施放火，非法携带管制刀具”为由分别处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天和<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，曾因所在辛庄村村主任郭世勋从金城石化公司往辛庄村的西北角运输化工废渣，污染土地，而向山东省各级环保部门举报，无果后，又于次日欲往北京环保部举报，随被县政府派人拦截并遭人毒打住院；过后其虽多次继续举报违法排污的村主任郭世勋，并要求警方尽快查处打人事件和为其被殴打导致常年半头痛后遗症做鉴定，但都被拒绝；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其再次被恒台县警方抓捕刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被淄博市桓台县法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，并被要求退赔相关经济损失<span lang="EN-US">2803</span>元。出狱后，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，因桓台县田庄镇文庄村的维权人士张岗遭抓捕，张岗之妹向其求助，其为营救张岗，遂不惧险境，多次向各级主管部门及新闻媒体举报、控诉恒台县公安局非法拘禁人，从而引社会热议；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，因维权者张岗已被批捕，其受张岗妹妹之托，立刻在微信群频繁发“紧急关注”，以呼吁更多正义人士关注张岗被捕事件；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，再次为声援张岗被抓事件而在新浪微博网站发文，揭露张岗所在田庄镇文庄村村委主任组织黑社会，贪污受贿、公账私存、挪用公款等渎职行为，因此文被人关注、转发近千次，遂立遭恒台县当局强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被恒台县警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”等再次刑拘，随后又被恒台县检察院很快以多项罪由正式批捕，并关押于桓台县看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，被淄博市恒台县法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”（<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月）、“妨碍公务罪”（<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月）、“敲诈勒索罪”（<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月）三罪，数罪并罚决定执行<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被山东省淄博市中级法院二审裁决：驳回上诉，维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US"> 2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。目前疑似在山东省淄博监狱（又称山东省第四监狱）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk52140367"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">耿潇男：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52140367;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年代出生，出版人，独立电视制作人，文化企业家，传奇天辉影视文化（北京）有限公司董事长，北京文化公共领域领军人物，公益文化思想活动策划<span lang="EN-US">/</span>执行<span lang="EN-US">/</span>传播者，中国在押政治犯。 耿潇男早年曾就读于中央戏剧学院，毕业后逐渐成为中国文化出版人，电影人，历任中国天画画天影业首席执行官、瑞雅书业总编辑，之后又和丈夫秦真共同创立传奇天辉影视文化（北京）有限公司，并担任董事长，随在业界知名度较高；近年来，因在北京文化公共领域以活跃、敢言着称，并积极致力于公益文化思想活动策划、执行及传播活动等，遂遭北京当局的维稳监控打压；<span lang="EN-US"> 2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，秦真<span lang="EN-US">/</span>耿潇男夫妇二人突然被警方带走，随后被北京市海淀区警方以涉嫌”非法经营罪“刑拘，现在北京市海淀区看守所关押；北京当局曾以经济问题为名调查其二人所属的出版公司，其丈夫与公司的账号均被查封；</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">多名好友均称其被抓捕，恐与此前公开为多名中国公共知识分子及异见人士发声呼吁有关，乃是因言获罪。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月遭正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US"> 2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日遭中共当局抓捕的著名媒体人耿潇男女士因言获罪被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑。后上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日二审维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日由北京市海淀区看守所转北京女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">耿宜敏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日出生，安徽省阜南县人，阜南县鹿城镇环北七路<span lang="EN-US">47</span>号公民，基督徒，安徽省阜南县基督教堂会堂主任，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，该基督教会接到当地县政府发来的欲拆除教会通知，声称政府要对阜南县富陂大道西侧实施棚改项目，而其教堂因位于该项目征收范围，所以需要拆除；因政府仅对其所在教会提出单方面拆迁补偿方案，并称若要异地重建政府将不予相应补偿，面对此单方武断决策，其及牧师、众信徒们认为明显有失公允，故遭到包括其在教会众教友的坚决反对，遂遭当局恶意报复与打压；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，当教堂众教友在做礼拜聚会时，突遭地方当局的强行闯入拆除，拆除时无任何合法文件及通知出示，且因事发突然，教堂财物来不及搬出，以致所有物品近都毁坏；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其与教会牧师、部分会堂成员数人被阜南县警方以涉嫌“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被阜阳县检察院予以正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其案在安徽省阜南县法院开庭受审；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被该法院一审以“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；其不服，提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，安徽省阜阳市中级法院经二审裁决，认为“原判认定的部分事实不清，证据不足”，故撤销原审，发回重审。目前被羁押于阜南县女子看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宫文义：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈尔滨市道外区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日哈尔滨市松北区公安分局绑架了宫文义等<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其他<span lang="EN-US">12</span>名法轮功学员被松北区检察院起诉。宫文义因身体原因保外回家，检察院称另案处理。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，宫文义在哈尔滨市江北住处，警察再次抓捕，并被抄家。后被在哈市第一看守所关押。后宫文义于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被哈市道外区法院秘密开庭并判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被押送哈市呼兰监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">巩进军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">曾因房屋遭遇强拆而上访多年，并屡遭截访，被遣返原籍；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因长期滞留北京上访，遂被送至黑监狱马家楼关押，后又被遣返原籍，途中其一行四人（均为访民）因遭到黑保安的非人虐待且拘不让饮食，故而在其人身自由及安全被“黑保安”非法严重侵害的情况下被迫予以正当防卫，双方发生激烈冲突，引发刺死黑保安事件（警方称一死一伤）；案发后河北省饶阳县警方迅速将其抓捕刑拘，并被关押在河北省衡水市深州看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被河北省衡水市中院以“故意伤害罪”判处无期徒刑；据悉其在被审讯时曾遭严重酷刑，仅一天即被电击<span lang="EN-US">50</span>余次。目前在河北省某监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">巩丽娜：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省锦州市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日晚，辽宁省锦州市法轮功学员何晓丹、王颖、巩丽娜同时被锦州市古塔公安分局及所辖派出所警察抓捕、抄家。她们最初被关押在锦州凌海隔离，之后被送到锦州市女子看守所关押。大约在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，她们被构陷到锦州市凌海检察院。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月获悉，她们三人都被凌海法院诬判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/25/457131.html#2322423213-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/25/457131.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">公丕荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东省沂南县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月生，家住沂南县花苑怡景。她于<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共迫害法轮功后，公丕荣曾被多次关押到看守所、洗脑班。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日早上<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点左右，公丕荣在做核酸检测的时候，突然遭到当地派出所<span lang="EN-US">110</span>警察的抓捕。同时，公丕荣家的两套楼房内的许多财物、物资被<span lang="EN-US">110</span>警察抄走。公丕荣被关押在临沂看守所。警察不让公丕荣的家人探视，连她家人送去的衣服也不让收。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月获悉公丕荣已经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/20/452141.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/20/452141.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贡觉尼玛（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1969</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州（以下简称阿坝州）若尔盖县人，西藏拉萨市哲蚌寺果芒学院经师，学者僧侣，中国在押良心犯。自幼成为僧侣，并长期进入西藏拉萨市哲蚌寺的果芒学院对佛教进修、研读；后因曾长期师从藏族著名佛学教师兰林仁波切（<span lang="EN-US">Lamrim<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>Rinpoche</span>），成其身边主要弟子，加之自身对佛学严谨博学的治学态度，故而被哲蚌寺果芒学院确立为经师（即精通佛教经藏的僧人，又称佛教讲经诵经的师父）；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，曾因藏区发生大规模以僧侣为主体，要求中共当局实现（或兑现）藏民族“自治独立”，并呼吁让达赖喇嘛回国返乡等政治诉求的抗议活动，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其所在寺庙约有<span lang="EN-US">350</span>名僧人亦积极参与其中，致使抗议活动态势迅速扩展到整个拉萨市区，以及四川、青海等藏区；针对此次抗议游行，中共西藏当局很快调拨大批持枪武警，因管控手段过于极端，遂导致双方发生对峙冲突，其间有不少僧人被抓捕，其余人等被送回寺庙严管看守；尽管此前其并未参加抗议游行活动，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其仍被拉萨市警方以涉嫌“抗议活动”抓走刑拘，自此失联；另有二名哲蚌寺好友、学者僧侣亦被一同抓捕；后其被拉萨市检察院正式批捕，理由是未能阻止哲蚌寺僧人举行大规模抗议行动；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，在被长期关押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年之久后，被拉萨市中级法院以不详罪名秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年，据悉，其辩护权遭剥夺，其狱中具体境况等信息不明。目前疑似在拉萨曲水监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贡却卓玛（藏）</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治区州阿坝县藏人，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因手中举着达赖喇嘛尊者的法相，在县城一处街道上和平游行，以此表达自己对达赖喇嘛尊者的崇敬，随立即被驻守在街道附近的中共警方拘捕。后音信全无。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">龚圣亮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">基督教牧师，华南教案首犯。龚圣亮牧师是湖北省枣阳市人，华南教会（<span lang="EN-US">SCC</span>）的创始人和领袖，该教派是中国一个家庭教会团契，在几个省份有<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万名信徒。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，龚圣亮在湖北省钟祥市被捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，他被湖北省荆门市中级法院裁定罪名成立，根据中国的反邪教法判处死刑。但由于国际压力，中国放弃了宗教罪名和死刑，并下令重新审判。中国湖北省高级法院后以事实不清、证据不足为由驳回了荆门市中级法院对基督教华南教会五名成员的死刑判决后，荆门市中级法院重新作出一审判决，把龚圣亮、徐福明、胡勇等三人改判无期徒刑，龚邦坤、李英改判<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年有期徒刑，原先在一审被判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年徒刑的向凤屏和刘先知等四人获当庭释放。一些作证反对龚的人后来表示，他们遭到了残酷的刑讯逼供。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">龚湘晖：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖南省长沙市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年生，财务人员，家住湖南省长沙市芙蓉区人民新村<span lang="EN-US">48</span>栋，<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年夏天开始修炼法轮大法，自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共发动对法轮功的迫害运动后，龚湘晖家就失去了安宁。龚湘晖及家人多次被抓捕、关押；多次被侵入住宅、搜查、被侵占财产。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被长沙市五里牌派出所警察抓捕，被关押在长沙市第四看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被浏阳市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，她被关押到湖南省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/9/451708.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/9/451708.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">龚月贵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北省武穴市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月出生，家住武穴市刊江办事处，目前被非法关押在黄冈市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日凌晨，武穴市公安局、田镇派出所、青林派出所、龙潭派出所同时出动，同一时间对郭平珍、龚月贵、刘艳峰、程学珍和廖元华五位法轮功学员的住宅、工作场所、法轮功学员及家人租借的房屋与仓库进行非法查抄，抄走法轮功书籍、资料、打印机、电脑等个人物品，并将五位法轮功学员抓捕，关押到看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，这五位法轮功学员被武穴市检察院非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，武穴市法院将五位法轮功学员判刑。郭平珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；龚月贵、刘艳峰和程学珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；廖元华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。龚月贵刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">古丽米拉•艾明（维吾尔）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1979</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，新疆维吾尔自治区人，原任职乌鲁木齐政府机关工作人员，网络作家，中国在押政治犯、良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年因在<span lang="EN-US">7</span>•<span lang="EN-US">5</span>事件发生时用手机短信向境外担任挪威维吾尔协会副秘书长的丈夫拜合提亚尔联系<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多次通报看到的情况，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被新疆乌鲁木齐市警方逮捕，据称在拘留期间曾遭受酷刑虐待；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被新疆乌鲁木齐市中级人民法院以“分裂国家、泄露国家秘密和组织非法示威”罪判处无期徒刑。此前曾在乌鲁木齐水磨沟女子监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日获悉，其在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年中共新疆当局录制的认罪悔过视频中，因曾签署了一份书面忏悔声明，遂其刑期被减为<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月；但因无法确认具体减刑日期，故其服刑到期日，暂不明晰；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">目前在乌鲁木齐市新疆第二监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/blog-post_99.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/blog-post_99.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">古丽仙•阿巴斯：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，新疆维吾尔自治区人，维吾尔族，退休医生，在押中国政治犯。被捕入狱前，为人生性善良、无私、正直，虽不热衷于参与政治，但有积极的奉献精神；自中共当局对新疆地区各少数族群（尤其是维吾尔族、哈萨克斯坦族人等）实行更严厉的高压管控以来，因其曾公开批评中共当局针对新疆维吾尔族等族群的人权不尊重、很糟糕，遂遭致新疆中共当局的强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，被新疆警方带走，自此失联；后经长达两年多的家人及国际人权组织机构连手查寻，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日终于获悉，其早被当地检察院以多项罪由予以批捕，指控其因“参与恐怖组织”、“恐怖活动”，其行为已严重地扰乱了社会秩序，故被抓捕、判刑；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，被新疆维吾尔自治区某法院以“恐怖组织罪”、“说明恐怖活动罪”和“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2038</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。目前服刑监狱缺详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谷明龙：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北保定市定州市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，谷明龙因到高蓬镇钮店村发放法轮功资料被定州市公安局抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月底被定州市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现被关押在唐山某监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">顾超：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">江苏省南京市溧水区法轮功学员。顾超<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年开始修炼大法。她在<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日讲真相时，被人诬告，被溧水区阳镇派出所抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被南京市雨花区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/23/%E6%B1%9F%E8%8B%8F%E7%9C%81%E5%8D%97%E4%BA%AC%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E9%A1%BE%E8%B6%85%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-441615.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/23/%E6%B1%9F%E8%8B%8F%E7%9C%81%E5%8D%97%E4%BA%AC%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E9%A1%BE%E8%B6%85%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-441615.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">顾聪：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">微信网名自由卫士，男，<span lang="EN-US">70</span>后人，山东人，居住济南市。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年期间因在<span lang="EN-US">twitter</span>发文反对过度防疫，反对独裁暴政，主张自由、民主、宪政，曾被其所在地派出所（济南市市中区王官庄派出所）限制在一个房间<span lang="EN-US">36</span>天，两次共抢走其三部手机。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日后其微信朋友圈停止更新，两部手机均打不通，后确认被王官庄派出所以辱骂国家领导人为由刑事拘留。后被正式逮捕，关押在山东省济南市（长青区）第三看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/blog-post_35.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/blog-post_35.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">顾秀芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，江西赣州法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">720</span>中共迫害法轮功以来，她不放弃大法修炼，去北京上访，坚持向世人、向政府官员讲法轮功，发送大法真相资料和《九评》等，先后<span lang="EN-US">12</span>次被抓、被关押或被诬判，其中<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次被劳教（累计<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年），也多次被抓捕在赣州看守所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日上午，章贡区公安局国保大队抓捕在家的顾秀芳，并抄了她的家，没有出示任何证件。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年年初被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/10/442548.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/10/442548.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">关兴涛</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：黑龙江省大庆市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日关兴涛与妻子吴艳华被抓捕、构陷，后被大庆市让胡路区法院判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。妻子吴艳华被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，现在被关押在黑龙江省女子监狱遭受迫害。关兴涛刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/2/26/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-421367.html#2122522533-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/2/26/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-421367.html#2122522533-1</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">官忠基：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省青岛市平度市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月平度市法院对法轮功学员官忠基判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，山东省青岛市法院又对官忠基上诉案维持原判。官忠基，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">66</span>岁，山东省平度市东阁办事处后巷子村人。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日下午，平度市七、八个警察到青岛李沧官忠基的儿子家将官忠基绑架到平度市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">桂敏海：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男，汉族，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日出生，原籍中国宁波，<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年加入瑞典国籍，“巨流传媒有限公司”股东。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月及<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月的中共特工赴香港、泰国实施的“香港铜锣湾书店案”震惊世界，共绑架了<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人，分别是桂敏海、林荣基、吕波、张志平、李波。后此<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人都于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年被中共逼迫在电视上认罪。桂敏海<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月中旬在央视称自己是为<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年前在宁波醉驾撞死人事件而潜返中国投案自首；<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，桂敏海又在电视镜头前承认自己非法偷运禁书进入大陆。后林荣基、吕波、张志平、李波相继被释放，唯有桂敏海遭扣押。中共当局一度声称桂敏海取保获释，实际上是仍遭秘密关押。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年被中共当局关押期间，中共称经其本人申请依法恢复中国国籍。宁波市中级法院于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日公开宣判，认定桂敏海犯为境外非法提供情报罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭春该</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：赵文静、黄金桔、吕月霞、郭春该及张迪<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">为涉</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省商丘巿宁陵县双庙村教会教案成员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日该教会一座兴建中的教堂，遭到数百名政府人员强拆，双方发生争执，教会物品被毁坏，信徒被打伤，数十人包括该<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名负责人被公安带走，后这<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被拘留。他们被指涉嫌“寻衅滋事”及“非法拘禁”罪，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被县检察院正式逮捕。其中张迪是临近一教会的传道人，为协助该教会建教堂，而遭牵连。目前，所有被捕者被羁押在宁陵县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，该教会成立<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，信徒百多人，当局曾要求加入三自教会不遂。目前此案音讯全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">郭春玲</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：黑龙江七台河市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1977</span>年生，女。一九九八年修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，七台河市茄子河区宏伟镇郭春玲与丈夫张广财、女儿张金凤、婆婆袁美娥，被哈尔滨市及七台河市公安局人员抓捕，从早八点到晚六点抄家，抢走大法书籍、打印机等。张金凤的一辆面包车也被强行开走。后获悉，郭春玲被七台河市茄子河区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/4/457381.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/4/457381.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郭丹霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖南省岳阳市石油公司退休会计、法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1948</span>年生。郭丹霞是于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被岳阳市楼区公安分局国保大队多个警察入室抓捕、抄家、审讯，后被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被检察院批捕，六月份被关押到岳阳市康复医院（精神病医院）。后郭丹霞被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，处罚金五千元。刑期自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郭飞雄：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本名杨茂东，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，湖北省谷城县人，律师，独立作家，著名人权活动家，新公民运动和南方街头运动积极参与者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，曾因申请反对日本右翼的“五四”抗议游行，而被北京市警方以涉嫌“聚众扰乱社会秩序”刑拘<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，又因参与广东省南海、佛山、番禺等地的民间维权工作，尤其是参与太石村罢免事件，提供法律援助，并在个人网页上网友通报太石村事件的进展信息，遂于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被广州省番禺市警方刑拘，直至<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日才获准释放。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，高智晟因发起绝食接力活动而被捕，郭飞雄展开营救活动，随即被广东警方以“非法经营罪”刑拘，并遭遇到包括“用电棍击打性生殖器”等方式的刑讯逼供；<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被广州市检察院正式起诉；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，被广州市天河区法院以“非法经营罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚款<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，因参与组织同年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-9</span>日在南方周末集团办公楼前围观声援南方周末职工抗议新年献词被改事件，以及<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，积极组织和促动八大城市街头举牌，敦促全国人大签署《公民权利和政治权利国际公约》活动，被当局视为是该活动的组织协调者之一，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被警方以涉嫌“众扰乱公共场所秩序罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被广州市天河区警方以同罪名正式逮捕，被关押于广州市天河区看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被广东省广州市天河区法院以“众扰乱公共场所秩序罪”、“寻衅滋事罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年；其不服上诉，后经广东省中级法院二审仍维持原判，随后送广东省阳春监狱和英德监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，因其长期流亡美国的妻子张青身患肠癌，生命垂危，随欲赴美给予照顾，熟料却在广州国际机场遭中共警方拦截、失联；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，再次赴美时在广州国际机场又被以“危害国家安全”为由抓捕、失联；其身患晚期癌症的妻子张青终等不到与丈夫见上一面，于美东时间<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日凌晨病逝，身边留下一儿一女；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，其被广州市警方以涉嫌「煽动颠覆国家政权罪」正式逮捕，且被禁止赴美国送别安葬刚刚病逝的妻子。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郭飞雄（杨茂东）于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被广州市公安局以涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权罪名移送广州市检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，获悉：自<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日著名人权捍卫者郭飞雄被抓捕至今，一直在绝食抗议中共当局对他的迫害，现其在狱中健康状况持续恶化。杨茂东（郭飞雄）案已经于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日由广州市人民检察院起诉至广州市中级人民法院，指控罪名为煽动颠覆国家政权（罪行重大），主要指控事实为三项：<span lang="EN-US">1. </span>杨茂东以郭飞雄为笔名在网络发表的文章；<span lang="EN-US">2. </span>创建“世界宪政民主论坛”网站并在该网站发表其本人及他人煽动颠覆国家政权的文章；<span lang="EN-US">3. 2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日欲赴美照料病妻被阻时接受自由亚洲电台的采访。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">目前被羁押于广州市第一看守所。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_1.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_1.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_94.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_59.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_59.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/blog-post_44.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">郭宏焱：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东胜利油田法轮功学员，女，胜利油田女职工。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，滨海公安局基地分局大肆抓捕了二十多位法轮功学员，其中包括正在单位上班的郭宏焱。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，东营市东营区法院对郭宏焱视频庭审，几天后宣判：郭宏焱被判三年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款两万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/24/458072.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/24/458072.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="background: white; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郭介仁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖南省益阳市资阳区新桥河镇新胜村村民。因土地维权持续上访要求解决村民基本医疗保障养老社保呼吁中共当局严惩新胜村村委、新桥河镇政府及益阳市资阳区区政府三级政府机构经办责任领导失职渎职、包庇纵容违法占地不法行为。郭介仁于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被益阳市公安局资阳分局刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月被以涉嫌强迫交易罪的罪名批捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郭立彬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省牡丹江海林市法轮功学员。郭立彬（郭立斌）和陈熙涛夫妇，家住牡丹江市海林市蔬菜村五队，是朴实的农民，以种菜为生。因为他们坚持修炼法轮大法，在中共疯狂迫害中，郭立彬和陈熙涛多次遭中共抓捕、关押。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，海林市国保大队将郭立彬和陈熙涛抓捕、关押。后郭立彬和陈熙涛夫妇均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，陈熙涛被劫持到黑龙江省女子监狱。郭立彬被关押在牡丹江监狱集训队迫。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/24/449999.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/24/449999.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭平珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北省武穴市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月出生，家住武穴市田镇，美容院老板，目前被非法关押在蕲春县拘留所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日凌晨，武穴市公安局、田镇派出所、青林派出所、龙潭派出所同时出动，同一时间对郭平珍、龚月贵、刘艳峰、程学珍和廖元华五位法轮功学员的住宅、工作场所、法轮功学员及家人租借的房屋与仓库进行非法查抄，抄走法轮功书籍、资料、打印机、电脑等个人物品，并将五位法轮功学员抓捕，关押到看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，这五位法轮功学员被武穴市检察院非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，郭平珍被取保回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，郭平珍在流亡中被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，武穴市法院将五位法轮功学员判刑。郭平珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；龚月贵、刘艳峰和程学珍被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；廖元华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。郭平珍刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭泉：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1968</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，江苏省南京市人，原南京师范大学副教授、研究生导师，中国大陆新民党创始人及代理主席，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年曾因发表公开信要求中国进行宪政改革，宣布组建“中国新民党”，主张在中国实行多党制和军队国家化等，遭受到中共当局的打压，<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被南京师范大学党委以违反宪法和教师法为由撤销其副教授职务，调任数据员；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，又因撰文批评中国政府处理四川地震的方式不当而被拘押<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，再次因其在网上发表<span lang="EN-US">300</span>多篇名为《民主先声》的文章，其中涉及组成以宣传民主思想为目标的新民党，以及提出以不合作方式进行公民行动的蓝色运动倡议等内容，被南京市警方刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被江苏省宿迁市中级人民法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，刑满释放。此前在江苏省南京市浦口监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，原南京师范大学副教授、南京著名人权捍卫者郭泉因关注湖北武汉疫情，为疫区人民发声而遭中共当局抓捕，随即被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，郭泉的母亲顾潇向媒体证实，郭泉本月中旬已经被南京检察院以“涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权罪”批捕。南京警方指郭泉在网络上发表了国情及疫情等信息大<span lang="EN-US">500</span>篇文章，其中半数是在煽动民众。斯伟江律师<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日在南京市第二看守所，会见郭泉。郭泉以煽动颠覆国家政权罪，在徐州市法院审理。对他指控，主要是微信上他的郭泉语录。郭泉满面红光，穿个短袖，身体健康。郭泉声言不惧坐牢。由徐州中院审理的郭泉煽动颠覆国家政权案，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分在南京市江宁区看守所开庭审理。郭泉的代理律师是郑州的常伯阳律师和上海的斯伟江律师。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，郭泉被中共当局以煽动颠覆国家政权罪判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/99.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/99.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/4_20.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/4_20.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">郭淑芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁锦州市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，女。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日郭淑芬被抓捕到锦州市北郊派出所，次日中午被关押到锦州市女子看守所。后凌海市检察院以所谓的“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”批捕郭淑芬。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，郭淑芬被庭审，后被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月后，郭淑芬向锦州中级法院提起上诉，锦州中级法院没有开庭审理就维持原判。现在被关押在辽宁女子监狱十二监区。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/7/458556.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/7/458556.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">郭秀海：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">福建省福州市永泰县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年五十九岁，是永泰县卫生局退休职工。她于一九九七年修炼法轮功。中共迫害法轮功后，郭秀海多次遭到骚扰、抄家、抓捕、关押等迫害。郭秀海<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月因讲真相被警察抓捕，后被长乐县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被劫持到福建女子监狱，现被关押在三监区八分监区，每月只允许消费一百元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/12/2022-6-12.html#zip4"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; text-underline: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b lang="EN-US">70</span>岁左右。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日晚，济南市铁路公安局、聊城市火车站派出所联合聊城市东昌府区国保大队、古楼派出所共十几个警察，闯入聊城市东昌府区法轮功学员华丽琴家中，把陈军、华丽琴、孙秀娥、李桂华、张亮、徐绍霞（<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁）和华丽琴的丈夫共<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人，抓捕到火车站派出所。火车站派出所对每位学员采指纹、勒索每人<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元保证金，同时在当晚和第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天分别对<span lang="EN-US">7</span>位法轮功学员及郭秀萍等抄家，抢走了大法书、真相资料和个人财物。第二天后取保候审。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日又遭抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/31/2021-8-31.html#zip7"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; 0pt;">河北</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">唐山法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">郭永凤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">贵阳法轮功学员，女，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1952</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年生，中国有色七冶一公司退休职工，家住贵阳市白云区。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，郭永凤在贵阳市观山湖区给民众发放法轮功资料时遭人恶告，被警察抓捕。后郭永凤被关押在贵阳三江看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月获悉，郭永凤被中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，已被关押到贵州省第一女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/13/457697.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">郭远和：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖南省桂东县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代生，女，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年约<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日上午，郭远和被桂东县<span lang="EN-US">610</span>李勇明带人，强行抢走她的袋子，其中有<span lang="EN-US">500</span>元现金和大法资料；随后<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被抄家，抢走家中所有的电脑、打印机、大量的现金、法轮功书籍等，家里的门被贴上封条。郭远和被关押在郴州看守所，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月份被庭审，被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。她现被关押在湖南省女子监狱高度戒备监区遭种种虐待，不让上厕所、侮辱谩骂、强制转化等折磨。她一度精神失常，被转入湖南省武警医院“治疗”，因灌食牙齿被撬掉<span lang="EN-US">8</span>颗，整个人瘦了一圈。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/13/446156.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/13/446156.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">郭元荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北省张家口市蔚县法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生。河北蔚县下宫村乡上宫村农民，原在大同市广灵县打工。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被保定市公安局直接通知山西省大同市公安局和河北省张家口市公安局抓捕，关押在大同市浑源县看守所。郭元荣被带到山西浑源县看守所后，出现严重病态，血压升高血糖升高，心动过速，三十天后被取保候审回家。后郭元荣被迫离家出走。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日在山西省大同市广灵县又被蔚县国保大队抓捕，被关押在大同市浑源县看守所。近日，家属获悉郭元荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/13/456730.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/13/456730.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">果然：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1981</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日出生，北京市朝阳区人，陕西省西安市南郊大学城自由生意人，政治异见人士，中国在押政治犯。近年来，因与友人经常在自己生意所在地聚会，自由讨论追求自由民主途径，被中共当局跟踪知晓，于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年二人被西安市长安区警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”抓捕刑拘，关押在西安市南郊三爻村看守所；之后因当局控其欲与他人密谋推翻中共政府，被西安市警方转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其案被陕西省西安市中级法院庭审，终被以“颠覆国家政权罪”一审重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；另一人士亦被重判，但缺详情；据悉，因其平素做事隐秘，而当局对其审判亦不公开，故而对其入狱详情几乎鲜为人知，直至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日陕西省渭南市中级法院在网上发布了一份“果然减刑刑事裁决书”才得知晓，渭南监狱鉴于其在狱中有悔过表现，积分较多，建议减刑，但渭南市中级法院却以“屡次严重违反监规被处分”为由拒不减刑，依旧刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。目前在陕西省渭南监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">果·喜饶嘉措：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1976</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日出生，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县人，知名藏族僧侣作家、学者和公共教育家，藏族持不同政见者，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。自幼即在四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县的格尔登寺（即该地区规模最大的藏传佛教格鲁派寺院）出家为僧，后又到西藏自治区拉萨市的哲蚌寺和色拉寺学习佛法，进行深造；曾因长期维护西藏地区的环境、宗教、语言和文化，以及出版过多本有关佛教哲学和西藏的传统、文化方面的书籍，而深受年轻一代藏民的喜爱与尊敬，但却引起中共当局的不悦、警觉和伺机迫害；<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾因参加反抗中共当局对阿坝地区僧侣强制实施的“爱国爱教”教育活动，而被四川当局拘捕，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，送四川省绵阳监狱服刑；曾在狱中受虐囚，且感染慢性肺病，至今未能治愈；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年奥运会在北京召开前，曾因藏区（主要是西藏拉萨）发生藏人大规模抗议游行事件，而又遭中共西藏当局拘捕，并被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，曾因发文批评中共政府镇压藏人同胞和实施高压强权残暴政策等，以及在青海省西宁市出版相关书籍，而再次被四川省国安局警方跨省拘捕，并被羁押于成都市某看守所；获释后，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2016</span>年，曾为继续致力于对藏传佛教文化进行研究和着书立说，而广游和拜访了藏区的多家寺院，并到广东中山大学学习西方哲学史等，此阶段，其行动尚且平安；但<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，当其在成都为以前狱中所患慢性肺病定期就医时，却被西藏自治区国安局警方以涉嫌“煽动分裂国家罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，其被西藏自治区拉萨市法院以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”开庭审判，至同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，终被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月获悉，其因在狱中遭酷刑虐待导致身体健康严重恶化，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，国际人权组织“人权观察”随发表声明，要求中共当局善待在押政治犯，立即无条件将其释放，让其获得尽快有效治疗。目前在拉萨市曲水监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/03/10.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/03/10.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt;
