11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈里斯别克·巴班（哈）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1987</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，新疆维吾尔自治区昌吉回族自治州呼图壁县人，哈萨克族，新疆乌鲁木齐市居民，哈萨克民歌手，中国在押良心犯。身为一哈萨克族歌手，因喜欢传唱民族歌曲而深受亲友及当地民众的好评；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，因曾到昌吉州吉木萨尔县泉子街镇吾塘沟村<span lang="EN-US">1</span>号参加表演，在表演会上演唱了“得罪中共当局”的歌曲，随遭到中共新疆当局的强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，被乌鲁木齐市警方以涉嫌“宣扬非法宗教等罪”抓捕，并被指控唱了政府认为“不该唱的歌曲”；据悉，自被捕后一直失联，家属不知其具体案情，只知至今尚未判刑，但又不被释放。目前被羁押于呼图壁县监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈木拉提<span lang="EN-US">.</span>吾甫尔</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：男，维吾尔族，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月出生，研究生医学博士，“国家长江学者创新团队发展计划”发起者，曾任“新疆医科大学校长”。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年曾入选中国科学院院士曾选初步候选人名单，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月任新疆食药监局局长。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，最后一次在媒体上露面。现被证实，已被乌鲁木齐警方以“传播极端民族主义思想”罪由被抓，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，香港中文大学和声书院学生会发表声明，声援曾经到访学校的哈木拉提·吾甫尔。后获悉，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被中共当局宣告「分裂国家罪」及「传播极端思想罪」成立，判处哈木拉提<span lang="EN-US">.</span>吾甫尔死刑，缓刑两年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈纳提别克•萨布尔别克（哈萨克）、哈伊拉提别克•木合塔尔汗（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">二人与</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">纳杂尔﹒叶尔江、阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克、乌木别提﹒卡斯木、沙部旦﹒沙伊合、耶尔肯别克﹒达列力、肯杰别克﹒达列力、玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗都是新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市巴里巴盖乡人，哈萨克族，穆斯林。其中，纳杂尔﹒叶尔江<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，乌木别提﹒卡斯木<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁，哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，沙部旦﹒沙伊合约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，耶尔肯别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，肯杰别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，因他们分别在私下里进行了穆斯林传统常规祷告仪式，而被中共新疆伊犁市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰当局知晓后拘捕，遂很快被阿尔泰市地方法院以“非法从事宗教活动”和“从事宗教极端活动”为由分别判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年不等刑期。目前各人具体判刑不详，刑至日期不详，服刑监狱不详，服刑状况及健康程度等不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">海拉提江·乌斯曼：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1958</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，新疆人，维吾尔族，维吾尔古典文学研究者，新疆维吾尔自治区政府科学文化研究所访问研究员，新疆大学维吾尔文学教授，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1978</span>年，曾就读于新疆大学维吾尔语文学系，至<span lang="EN-US">1982</span>年毕业；后在新疆乌鲁木齐市的新疆大学长期任职，并致力于对维吾尔族古典文学的研究和撰写工作；曾撰写过<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多部书籍和<span lang="EN-US">100</span>篇学术论文，并参加过数十次国际学术会议；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，曾因参加在土耳其的布尔萨举行的研讨会，并在会上讨论了维吾尔文化，随被中共新疆当局关注，后于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年被定为搞“分裂主义宣传”；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，因曾在日本一所大学讲课，课堂上使用的例子被中共当局视为“对中国文化的排斥”，并曾应邀参加了一次土耳其的突厥学会议，遂被乌鲁木齐市警方刑事拘留；后又被转正式逮捕，并被指控在其研究中，因过度赞扬维吾尔文化，而“在几代维吾尔学生中，灌输分裂主义意识形态”，随有搞“分裂主义”活动之嫌；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，被新疆乌鲁木齐市法院以“分裂主义”罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。目前在新疆乌鲁木齐市一家监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/10.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/10.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">海莱提•尼亚孜（维吾尔）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1960</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，新疆维吾尔自治区塔城市人，原《新疆法制报》总编室主任、《法治纵横》杂志社副社长、《新疆经济报》前记者，原“维吾尔在线”网站的编辑和管理员以及维吾尔在线论坛版主，维吾尔著名媒体人，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，乌鲁木齐<span lang="EN-US">7</span>•<span lang="EN-US">5</span>事件后因多次接受包括香港《亚洲周刊》在内的采访，分析新疆骚乱的深层次原因，批评时任自治区书记王乐泉治理政策不当，并透露自己曾经在<span lang="EN-US">7.5 </span>前一天向新疆领导部门提出过预警却未被采纳等，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被警方从乌鲁木齐家中抓走，关押在乌鲁木齐天山看守所；<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日其家人收到当局的拘捕通知书，随后被乌鲁木齐法院以“危害国家安全罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年。现在新疆昌吉监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">海米提·阿不都热合曼（维）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1954</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州伊宁市人，维吾尔族名<span lang="EN-US">HaimitiAbudureheman</span>，原伊犁州邮电局退休干部，中国在押良心犯。被捕前从未参与过政治维权或请愿活动，为人忠厚老实，深得其子女的爱戴及信任；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，曾与妻子沙阿呆提<span lang="EN-US">.</span>巴吴顿二人到土耳其旅行，并与已在瑞典流亡且参与政治维权和申请了政治庇护的儿子托格鲁克·海米提见过面，返回新疆时，因当时新疆并未出现“政治再教育营”之说，故其行踪随被当局知晓，但并未被伊宁市警方问讯或传唤训诫，就此二人一直相安无事；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年，随着中共当局在新疆出现大规模清理少数民族宗教文化行动以来，新疆各地越来越多的推出了“政治思想再教育营”（又称“政治再教育中心”）计划，其曾经出国探亲之举（即曾与成为政治难民的儿子见面），使其即刻变成当局仇视和需要严打报复的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，其夫妇二人双双被伊犁哈萨克自治州伊宁市警方带走，并送某“政治再教育中心”羁押，自此失联；<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，知其被伊宁市警方以“与在海外申请政治庇护的儿子会面”为罪由逮捕，近期被新疆伊犁州伊宁市法院重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年，罪名不详，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2035</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日；</b>据悉，其在看守所内身体健康状况极差；其在乌鲁木齐市一家银行工作的女儿遭牵连，亦于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被强制送进“政治再教育中心”接受洗脑式教育，至今下落不明。目前服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郝虎成：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年生，河北省邯郸市武安市活水乡马店头村人，法轮功学员。在北京市以修理空调电器为生。郝虎城曾于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年在浙江宁波打工期间向世人讲述法轮功真相时被抓捕，被浙江省宁波法院判刑两年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年过年期间，郝虎城通过微信向（大纪元）记者发送了<span lang="EN-US">1</span>段拜年视频。正月初<span lang="EN-US">6</span>，北京市国保警察通过微信软件及收寄快递地址定位后电话联系了郝虎城，由于正月期间郝虎城回原籍老家过年，北京市国保责令武安市活水乡派出所对郝虎城实施管控。活水乡派出所遂签发了对郝虎城拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天的拘留证，因郝虎城提出要请北京律师复议，派出所未执行拘留。农历<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月初，郝虎城再次去北京打工。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日晚，郝虎城在北京市城区开汽车途中，遭警察手机定位拦截、搜查，警察从郝虎城的车里发现了<span lang="EN-US">1000</span>张<span lang="EN-US">5</span>元面值的真相币，然后闯到郝虎城的租住屋中将郝虎城的手机、存折等私人物品抄走。当晚，郝虎城被抓捕至北京市昌平区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初，北京市昌平区法院判决郝虎城<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/28/%E6%B2%B3%E5%8C%97%E6%AD%A6%E5%AE%89%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E9%83%9D%E8%99%8E%E5%9F%8E%E9%81%AD%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-441846.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/28/%E6%B2%B3%E5%8C%97%E6%AD%A6%E5%AE%89%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E9%83%9D%E8%99%8E%E5%9F%8E%E9%81%AD%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-441846.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郝劲松：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山西“知名法律人士”。郝劲松生于<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年，山西忻州人。著名人权律师。郝劲松律师自<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年开始先后<span lang="EN-US">7</span>次将国家税务总局、北京地铁运营公司、北京铁路局告上法庭，原他因对“打破行业‘霸王条款’起到了一定作用”而入选“<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年构建经济和谐十大受尊崇人物”。郝劲松被先后提名为<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>中国法制新闻人物，<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年度十大法制人物，并以“维权战士”的身份写入《<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>中国法治蓝皮书》。因介入推动铁道部春运不涨价案件入选《<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>中国法治蓝皮书》，并当选<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>中国十大消费维权人物，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年因介入陕西华南虎案件和杨佳案被《南方人物周刊》评选为“中国魅力人物——公义之魅”。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，介入上海“钓鱼执法事件”。后成立山西定襄县劲松法务咨询中心。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，郝劲松向定襄县环保局实名举报当地的诚泰纺织印染公司涉嫌污染空气和水源。郝劲松于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日就连续两天遭到户籍地山西省定襄县晋昌镇派出所以“寻衅滋事”为由传唤后，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日再遭该派出所传唤。随后被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，行政拘留期满被转刑事拘留，控罪为涉嫌寻衅滋事。后遭正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，郝劲松在原先被控涉嫌寻衅滋事罪和诽谤罪之外，被加控诈骗罪，后起诉。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郝劲松被涉嫌诽谤罪、寻衅滋事罪、诈骗罪案，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9:00</span>在山西省定襄县人民法院审判庭开庭。庭审仅在中午休庭两个半小时以后，于当晚<span lang="EN-US">20:00</span>庭审结束，法庭没有当庭宣判表示会择期宣判。郝劲松是在看守所视频参与庭审，据仅仅被允许参加旁听的两个家属所见，郝劲松的精神状态很好，对法院指控的罪名不予认可。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_96.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_96.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郝鸣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省籍人，基督徒，四川省德阳市秋雨青草地归正教会前长老（即退休长老），成都市秋雨圣约教会牧者、传道人，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月起，因中共当局对不同意识形态的打压，尤其是针对自由宗教信仰者和追求者的打压日趋严厉，随其退休之前所在的德阳市秋雨青草地教会频遭当局骚扰与逼迫；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">又因此教会拒不配合德阳市民宗局了解教会奉献的收入情况，拒绝撕下教会窗外“爱耶稣”字样的标识等，故而教会信众尽被当地派出所警方强行核对户口与地址，被街道办事处成员上门询问相关聚会问题，被小区网格化管理工作人员（简称“网格员”）上门登记会友情况，被国保警方约谈布道所需的植堂者等等；在此期间，其虽然已从德阳秋雨青草地归正教会退休，但因其心系教会，又在成都秋雨圣约教会继续挂职，传讲福音，随立遭四川当局的警觉与监视；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，成都秋雨圣约教会突遭成都警方的大抓捕，王怡牧师夫妇及秋雨圣约教会的覃德富、李英强等 多名长老、牧者和同工（即教会神职服侍人员）百余人尽被成都警方以涉嫌<span lang="EN-US">"</span>煽动颠覆国家政权罪<span lang="EN-US">"</span>或<span lang="EN-US">"</span>非法经营罪<span lang="EN-US">"</span>刑拘<span lang="EN-US">;</span>后因打压扩大化，同年<span lang="EN-US">12 </span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-12</span>日，其之前所在德阳市秋雨青草地教会亦受冲击， 教会会堂被德阳市旌阳区警方与辖区城北街道办、小区等多方工作人员连手闯入，正在查经的信徒遭驱离，教会正常的敬拜聚会遭取缔，提供教会租用房屋的房东也遭警方施压作笔录，被要求立即撕毁与教会签订的房屋租赁合同，并让教会即刻搬离会堂场所；因其等教会牧者、长老与同工拒绝了当局这一无理要求，表示仍将继续进入会堂敬拜，遂其等神职人员之后频遭当局跟踪、监控和严打；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，因曾参与了已被重判的王怡牧师发起的《牧者联署：为基督信仰的声明》，同时又与贵州省贵阳市仁爱教会长老张春雷（现已被贵州当局抓捕）、四川省德阳市青草地教会长老武见男等人敢于公开支援王怡牧师和乐于帮助成都秋雨教会，随遭遇更进一步逼迫打压；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，与德阳青草地教会现长老武见男夫妇、教会同工刘五一、刘永波、蓝恩光等人被四川省德阳市旌阳区警方抓走，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其与武见男 长老被以涉嫌<span lang="EN-US">"</span>诈骗罪<span lang="EN-US">"</span>正式刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24 </span>日，其被德阳市旌阳区检察院以同罪由转正式批捕。目前被羁押于德阳市看守所（四川省德阳市双东镇龙凤村，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">618017</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"></span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/blog-post_84.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/blog-post_84.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郝明静：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北民营企业主，因上访被判刑，现被政府囚禁在精神病院。郝明静是因为其投资开办的沙厂被抢而上访，屡屡遭到政府与公安的维稳“铁拳”的打击，还以“寻衅滋事罪”对其判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。郝就为这冤事上访，襄州区政府就灭绝人性迫害他。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，政府和公安非法把他关进了襄州黄集镇静怡精神病医院，关了一个月零<span lang="EN-US">18</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，政府又把郝明静转送到襄阳市精神病的安定医院，强迫他吃精神病药，不吃，就把他捆绑去座老虎凳强行灌药，非要把他治成精神病，还逼迫他的儿子签字。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月郝明静的女儿，因为父亲失踪两个多月了没有音讯，就根据从其他渠道获得的信息，偷偷进入襄阳市精神病的安定医院，探望了被囚禁于此的老父亲郝明静。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/blog-post_98.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/blog-post_98.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郝淑娥：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，黑龙江省密山市人，黑龙江省密山市<span lang="EN-US">855</span>农垦小区<span lang="EN-US">B</span>区三委<span lang="EN-US">56</span>栋<span lang="EN-US">4</span>号居民，密山市<span lang="EN-US">855</span>农场工人，维权访民中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，曾因其兄被人莫名伤害致死，割破塑料连体渔衣，沉尸水库，其虽紧急报案请求警方勘察和能给予一个公正说法，但因嫌犯大有背景，故当地警方竟从最初尸检报告表明是被击打致死，改为再次尸检又称是溺水而亡。又因当局拒其聘请的法医参与尸检，为求公道，其被迫冰尸十多年，上访十多年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">后因其在上访过程中帮助过许多与其类似的维权访民，并积极参与公益事件，随遭当局逼迫打压，被公安部定为一级维稳临控对象。曾因在家乡多次上访投诉无果，只好进京信访，但又遭进一步的维稳打压。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，曾因以唱歌方式述说其兄被害冤情而被北京警方以涉嫌“扰乱社会公共秩序罪”刑拘于北京市丰台区看守所，<span lang="EN-US">32</span>天之后才得取保获释。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，又因曾与多名维权访民在北京西单乞讨而被北京西城区警方刑拘，羁押于北京市西城区看守所<span lang="EN-US">31</span>天后才获释放。同期，因其长期驻京信访，而曾被黑龙江截访办人员密押于北京市东城区的一处黑监狱。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，再次在北京被警方刑拘，后被黑龙江省鸡西市密山市检察院以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”予以批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年底，检方曾派两人到看守所对其恐吓，要求其与嫌犯方金钱私了案件，否则将以“敲诈勒索罪”对其量刑，但被其断然拒绝。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，因其在看守所内一直坚称“不要一分钱，只要还案件真相，无惧坐牢”，故而当地警方要其交保释金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元即可取保释放，但被其再度拒绝，并对警方声明：要么无罪释放，要么继续坐牢。目前被羁押于黑龙江省鸡西市密山市看守所。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/855_14.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/855_14.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">郝志娓：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年出生，山西省籍人，湖北省鄂州市鄂城区居民，基督徒，鄂州市鄂钢桥家庭教会牧师，中国在押良心犯。早年曾就读于湖北武汉的中南神学院（由豫、鄂、湘、粤、桂、琼等省市基督教协会合办）；<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年毕业后，曾被邀请到湖北省鄂州市“三自”爱国会教堂讲道，并因讲道效果好，深得信徒赞许，故而最终成为教堂的专职神职人员；后因其不认同宗教局管理，将其所在教会从“三自”变为“非三自”，遂其牧师身份一直未经鄂州市宗教局审批认证；之后其教会被官方取缔，但其依旧在原址教堂聚会讲道，并于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年按照家庭教会的传统惯例，由<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名牧师按立成为牧师，此外，教会的奉献款由几个主要同工进行管理和支出（含教会的日常支出、奉养牧师和支持别的传道人等）；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，曾因当地政府对鄂钢桥教会的教堂提出拆迁要求，被信徒拒绝，故而鄂州市民宗局曾发《告知书》要求其等配合政府拆迁，但因同年其丈夫患肝癌去世而需打理家事，故长时间未去教堂也未能及时与民宗局沟通；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，其与两位教会同工突然被鄂州市鄂城区警方抓捕，其中，其被以涉嫌“诈骗罪”刑拘，另两人分别被以“诈骗罪”和“阻碍公务罪”刑拘，并都被关押于鄂州市第一看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其等被当地鄂城区检察院以同罪名予以批捕，指控其等因在未经基督教两会批准的情况下，擅自传道和收取奉献金等，故此行为已涉嫌诈骗罪，应予逮捕、判刑；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，另两位同工在被超期关押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年之后，终获取保释放，但其仍被续押不放；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，其案在湖北省鄂州市鄂城区法院一审正式开庭审理，至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，终被该法院以“诈骗罪”枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日；据悉，自其被抓捕后，其上初中的小儿子摩西出现了严重的抑郁症倾向，并于当年辍学一年；而其因长期超押遭迫害，曾在看守所得了<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次急性胰腺炎，幸得 急救，险些丧命。目前疑似在湖北省鄂州监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日二审驳回上诉，维持原判。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/8.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/8.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">韩建海：男，</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁，辽宁省大连市沙河口区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日晚九点左右，张仁光、王尚杰、韩建海、李静波<span lang="EN-US">,4</span>人因发真相资料，分别被国保和民权派出所绑架。在张仁光家抄走大量耗材。后全送姚家看守所。大连市沙河口区法院<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日庭审法轮功学员张仁光、王尚杰、韩建海、李静波，并判韩建海<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">韩建平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林长春法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生。老家山东的，骨子里有山东人的那股倔劲儿。韩建平于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日在家中被四平、梨树公安绑架构陷抓捕，一直被关押在四平市看守所。后获悉其于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被中共判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">韩立萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北省承德市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生，女。其于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被承德市公安局双桥分局政保大队警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，家属收到逮捕通知书，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，承德市双桥区法院对其判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/13/458755.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: Roman&quot;;">河南政府信息公开申请人、知名民间维权举报打假人王清同案。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被南阳市卧龙区警方以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，本案被南阳市卧龙区检察院移交至南阳市卧龙区法院进行起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其王清、陈强、王聚才及韩猛<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人被以涉“敲诈勒索案”在南阳市卧龙区法院开庭受审，后韩猛被该法院一审以“敲诈勒索罪”枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，韩猛刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">韩仁义：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西大同法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，韩仁义在大同市明堂公园向行人发放法轮功被迫害小册子，被人诬告。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，韩仁义在东信国际四号馆前讲法轮功，被警察抓捕后抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，韩仁义被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/20/449839.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/20/449839.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">韩淑娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女士，天津市河东区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，韩淑娟被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月中旬，韩淑娟发放真相资料，被抓捕，后又被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，韩淑娟在天津市河东区太阳城小区讲法轮功，遭恶人诬告，被天津市河东区公安分局鲁山道派出所抓捕，关押在天津市河东区看守所。后韩淑娟被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，被关进天津女子监狱。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日因街上宣传法轮功被天津市河东区公安分局抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被河东区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">韩淑云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">天津市宁河区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生，女。因修炼法轮功，在过去的二十多年中，韩淑云坚持信仰法轮功真、善、忍，多次遭抓捕、关押、被迫流离失所，以及持续的骚扰。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日晚，天津芦台派出所伙同国保十多人，闯入韩淑云的家，将她抓捕，并抄家。后得知，韩淑云被宁河区公检法人员暗箱构陷、判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被关押到天津女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/17/458894.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/17/458894.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">韩晓栋</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，山西省临汾市人，基督徒，临汾市基督教圣约家园教会传道人，中国在押良心犯。因其所在教会属于基督教归正家庭教会，且因其与李洁等神职人员及教会众信徒拒不愿接受中共“三自”教会的管控，遂自新宗教事务条例实施以来，即成为屡遭逼迫的家庭教会之一；在逼迫中，不仅教会时常被民宗局官员带着多人前来骚扰、威胁和冲击，其及其他教会传道和同工等亦成为山西当局伺机打压的维稳对象；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，因其教会在户外举办<span lang="EN-US">70</span>人的“亲子营”活动，遂突遭当地警方<span lang="EN-US">100</span>余人的围堵和冲击，并将包括其在内的所有现场参与者悉数带走，同时扣押所有人员的手机、计算机、硬盘、投影仪、凳子、汽车等物品；之后虽有部分小孩被送回，但所有成人均被扣留，且其本人住处遭查抄，将其部分书籍数据等搜走；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天之后的<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，其及同是教会神职人员的李洁等人被派出所警方带走，并均被临汾市公安局直属分局警方以涉嫌“诈骗罪”指定居所监视居住；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，其与李洁二人被山西省临汾市警方以涉嫌“诈骗罪”转为刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其与李洁又被临汾市检察院以同罪名正式批捕。目前被羁押于山西省尧都区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/blog-post_49.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/blog-post_49.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">韩燕雷：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽省人，基督徒，安徽省芜湖市基督教某家庭教会事工人员，教会学校老师，中国在押良心犯。因信仰基督，并在安徽省芜湖市基督教一家庭教会的教育学堂事工当老师，随遭中共安徽当局在意识形态方面的强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被闯入教学点的芜湖市戈江区警方将包括其在内的<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名老师莫名抓走，同时，教学点遭查抄，内中一切物品均被扣押，后其<span lang="EN-US">10</span>人被视为同案嫌疑人统一被芜湖市戈江区警方以涉嫌“非法经营罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初，除杨志言等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>名老师被准予取保候审外，韩燕雷及王明海等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人被芜湖市戈江区检察院以涉嫌“非法经营罪”转正式批捕；据悉，其案已有律师代理。目前被羁押于芜湖市第一看守所（安徽省芜湖市戈江区火龙岗镇白马山村，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">241000</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">韩震昆：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">云南昆明法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年生，原云南省网球运动队队员，<span lang="EN-US">1991</span>年转业到昆明锦华大酒店做服务员，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年，因修炼法轮功被迫辞职。韩震昆因修炼法轮功，曾经两次被抓捕，入冤狱<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年。此次是韩震昆自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年“<span lang="EN-US">7</span>•<span lang="EN-US">20</span>”中共迫害法轮功以来第<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，韩震昆送<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名装修工人到西双版纳州景洪市，在装修工程完工，要返回昆明时，由于勐腊县勐龙镇景龙村中共党支部书记岩温恶意报警，景洪市国保警察以监控里怀疑韩震昆发放大法法轮功资料，在景洪东风农场永安宾馆内将韩震昆抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，韩震昆被勐腊县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">何斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北维权人士<b>。</b><span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，湖北维权人士何斌、徐彩虹夫妇的家人一大早收到襄阳市樊城区分局的拘留通知书，称何斌、徐彩虹夫妇俩涉嫌寻衅滋事犯罪已被刑事拘留。何斌、徐彩虹夫妇俩是<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日早上被从家中传唤走的，下午家人前去辖区派出所询问，派出所告知人已经被带走了。何斌、徐彩红夫妻因为租赁纠纷案件一直在北京信访，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被从北京截访人员接回去的，回家后住了一宿再被传唤，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日家人收到刑事拘留通知书。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/blog-post_10.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/blog-post_10.html</span></b></a></span><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">何方美：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，河南省新乡市辉县人，网名“十三妹”，“疫苗宝宝之家”维权团体发起人，人权捍卫者，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年度“曹顺利人权捍卫者奖共同获得者，中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日其年仅<span lang="EN-US">1</span>岁<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月龄的小女打了百白破疫苗之后导致全身瘫痪，其多方求助投诉均被拒，遂逐级维权讨说法，后因多地亦发生类似疫苗伤害宝宝事件，随组建“疫苗宝宝之家”维权团体共同呼吁，以求当局关注并给予合理赔偿救治；然当局却对此一拖再拖，其被迫到北京上访，故屡遭抓捕打击；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，因中共两会期间与各地问题疫苗家长到北京王府井为残儿募捐，随被新乡市辉县警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，又被以辉县警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”转刑拘，关押在河南省新乡市看守所；因期间一直拒绝认罪，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被新乡市辉县检察院以同罪名批捕，后被起诉并罗列<span lang="EN-US">6</span>项罪，建议量刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其案在河南省辉县法院正式开庭；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，又被辉县检察院以“事实不清、证据不足”为由撤诉，后被无罪获释；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，因其不断发声请求国家立法解决疫苗问题、呼吁联合国关注中国疫苗问题等，而在北京再度遭遇强迫失踪；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">释放后，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，因当地政府阻挠其带疫苗致残的女儿看病，随对辉县政府招牌泼墨抗议，而被行政拘留；后于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日第二次对辉县市政府泼漆抗议；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，知其及其丈夫、六岁的儿子、三岁的残疾女儿一起被警方软禁，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，其被河南省辉县市警方以涉嫌“重婚罪”和“寻衅滋事罪”正式逮捕；据悉，羁押期间，其产下一女，有关部门已致电其家属，称若不去领回孩子，其所有孩子将被送到福利院。目前被羁押于河南省新乡市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，河南辉县警察骗遭软禁的何方美说快要放她了，带她出去拍照体检，结果第二天直接把何方美带去参加庭审。她被当庭逮捕。其亲属接到逮捕通知后立刻聘请了律师。可律师来辉县法院时，法院以案件已经开过庭，审判委员会已经讨论过了为由，拒绝律师阅卷。辉县法院连律师阅卷都不准许，本案谈何公正处理？何方美多年来致力于疫苗群体维权。其实她自己也有听力残障，即天生没有耳廓、耳洞，需要大声或者看唇语来跟别人交流。本案在辉县法院开庭时，法院只让她听审，拒绝她看任何书面材料。她当庭才知丈夫李新被以寻衅滋事罪、重婚罪判了<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年多，已在服刑中。何在开庭时解除了法援律师，提交了<span lang="EN-US">50</span>页的自辩词。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/202275.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/202275.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_63.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_63.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">何观娇：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日晚，何观娇和妹妹何水姑到福州动车北站，买了<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>号（大年二十九）早上<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点<span lang="EN-US">10</span>分由福州北站来往北京西的动车。等待到第二天（<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>号）早上离动车发车的前半个小时，何氏姐妹俩在福州火车站南广场，被一帮人共计六个人强行绑架到一辆白色私家车上。今年已经<span lang="EN-US">54</span>岁的何观娇，是上世纪七十年代因中越关系恶化而跟父母归国的侨民。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年到<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，何观娇分别在深圳市宝安区公明镇摩打制造厂和深圳市飞狮电子工业有限公司工作，因为长期接触有毒胶水，导致呼吸困难，多次昏倒，差一点死掉。何观娇多次要求用人单位调换工种被拒绝，加上得不到积极治疗，终失去劳动能力，被用人单位赶出厂门，到劳动仲裁部门要求进行工伤鉴定，被拒绝，遂开始了上访之路。由于何观娇在福州市晋安区新店镇横厝<span lang="EN-US">24</span>号<span lang="EN-US">20</span>座<span lang="EN-US">302</span>（福州北郊华侨塑料二厂）的房屋又遭强拆，且没有得到政府的任何安置，一直借住在姐姐妹妹家中。为了维护自己的合法权益，何观娇趁春节乘车方便，遂于大年二十九购买动车票，准备再次进京信访，却遭绑架失踪。后获知其被关在福州神康精神病院。在何水姑跟福州神康精神病院医生通电话过程中，被告知是公安将其强制送到精神病院的。至今仍未释放。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">何国熬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖北省咸宁市通城县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1948</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被抓捕，关押到通城县看守所，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日他被转到沙洋范家台监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/26/459213.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/26/459213.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">何丽霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江大庆市杜蒙县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共疯狂发动了对法轮功的迫害，何丽霞因讲法轮功真相，曾<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次被中共劳教，有<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被迫害差点失去生命。这场迫害给何丽霞造成家庭破裂，幼小的女儿在失去妈妈的痛苦中长大。何丽霞迫流离失所近两年，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月回家才<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月左右，再<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被恶警抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日何丽霞再次被抓捕，关押在大庆市第二看守所。当天，大庆市、区、县有<span lang="EN-US">60</span>多名法轮功学员被抓捕，多数被抄家，<span lang="EN-US">20</span>来人被送进大庆市看守所关押，十多人被送拘留所关押。何丽霞在看守所绝食抗议关押迫害，<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天后出现生命危险，国保警察找家人签字，办了“取保候审”。几天后，国保又找何丽霞，要所谓“走法律程序”，图谋对她判刑迫害。何丽霞被迫流离失所两年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，何丽霞在回家刚<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个多月，再次被恶警抓捕，被关押在杜蒙县看守所，后关押到大庆看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月份，何丽霞被大庆市让胡路法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，现关押到哈尔滨女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/26/2021-9-26.html#zip3"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/26/2021-9-26.html#zip3</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">何莲春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">云南省红河州蒙自市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年出生在石屏县宝秀镇，后嫁到蒙自县文澜镇高家村。此前何莲春曾接连两次遭冤判共<span lang="EN-US">17</span>年，在狱中熬过了<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，出狱后她到昆明打工，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月份又被警察抓捕、构陷，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。 何莲春<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，她与其他四名法轮功学员在蒙自城区贴法轮功真相资料时，被「<span lang="EN-US">610</span>」（专门迫害法轮功的非法机构）国保警察构陷，于<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被红河州中级法院判重刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，提前<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半出狱。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，她再次被蒙自县「<span lang="EN-US">610</span>」抓捕到洗脑班「转化」迫害，由于她不放弃修炼，又被红河州中级法院判重刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。服刑期间何莲春曾遭酷刑虐待。在<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日何莲春被送入云南省第二女子监狱，关押在六监区期间，严管达五年多。期间，她被罚坐「小凳子」（长约<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多公分、宽约<span lang="EN-US">8</span>公分多），不准洗澡、洗衣，一天只给一瓶水（<span lang="EN-US">500ml</span>），近一年被限制次数上卫生间，而且经常遭到包夹（监管法轮功学员的刑事犯）的殴打、穿「紧束衣」、两次被开批斗会侮辱。何莲春进行了二十多次绝食抗议，遭到上百次野蛮灌食、灌药，饭食里投放不明药物。每次插胃管都是从她鼻子里硬插，导致她满鼻腔、满嘴都是血，每次她都要吐很多的血。由于插的次数多了，她的鼻腔、口腔、喉咙粘膜溃烂，吞咽非常困难。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月才刑满出狱。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，何莲春去探望法轮功学员王汇真，在返回住地的途中，被追到昆明来的蒙自市国保大队警察抓捕，说是为中共<span lang="EN-US">70</span>年「建国」阅兵维稳。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，她被建水县检察院非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，何莲春被构陷到法院。她的所谓「罪行」是：她去看法轮功学员王汇真后，被抓捕时，一部手机被查获，里面存有法轮功资料。因此被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">何萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林松原市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日上午，何萍从母亲家回来，刚走进居民小区就被松原市国保大队抓捕、抄家。警察抄走电脑一台、真相手机五部、电话卡二十多张和所有大法书籍。后被刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。关押在松原市看守所一年之多后，现<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">何清香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东梅州法轮功学员，女。十年多来，因修炼法轮功，何清香与丈夫涂晴光多次遭迫害，夫妻俩曾于<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被抓捕，而后都被原判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，涂晴光于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月结束冤狱从梅州监狱出狱回家；何清香于次月从广东省女子监狱出狱回家。夫妻俩团聚不到<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日上午，涂晴光在梅江区东郊派出所附近的客家公园讲真相时，被东郊派出所警察抓捕。同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，他被梅江区法院判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半刑，于<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被劫持到广东省韶关监狱继续迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日早上<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点左右，何清香在出门上班时，被蹲坑的国保及金山派出所警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US"> 2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年并勒索<span lang="EN-US">6</span>万元罚金。据悉，她已于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被劫往广东省女子监狱继续关押迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/15/%E5%B9%BF%E4%B8%9C%E6%A2%85%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E4%BD%95%E6%B8%85%E9%A6%99%E8%A2%AB%E5%8A%AB%E6%8C%81%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-441305.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/15/%E5%B9%BF%E4%B8%9C%E6%A2%85%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E4%BD%95%E6%B8%85%E9%A6%99%E8%A2%AB%E5%8A%AB%E6%8C%81%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-441305.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">何善航：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2000</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，香港油尖旺区人，香港理工大学毕业生，香港某国际知名公司职员，香港逃犯条例修订草案（民间和媒体俗称“送中条例”、“逃犯条例”或“引渡条例”）反对者，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>·<span lang="EN-US">1</span>尖沙咀抗议者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，因中共当局在香港推出“逃犯条例修订草案”，遭到香港民众普遍反对，遂掀起“反送中”运动，并由香港民间人权阵线发起「没有国庆，只有国殇」之游行，以期在庆祝中华人民共和国成立<span lang="EN-US">70</span>周年大会期间同步进行示威，由港岛铜锣湾游行至中环，向港府公开表达反对“逃犯条例修订草案”的要求，但却遭到香港警方的明确反对，并被公众集会及游行上诉委员会上诉后被驳回；熟料港府官方的这一反对立场和决定立即激怒了要求高度自治，“真普选”、“真自由”的香港民众的强烈反对，遂有大批民众决定自我承担法律后果，在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日国庆节当天，在港多区自行发起“反对逃犯条例修订草案”示威抗议行动；何善航因支持“反送中”运动，故在此过程中亦积极参与了从尖沙嘴到油麻地一带的抗议示威，但因抗议过程中诸多香港民众与前来镇压的港警发生了严重的暴力冲突，遂遭港警的实弹打压，最终有多人被实弹打伤和被抓捕，其中，何善航等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被以“参与暴力”之名强行拘捕；后其等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被警方以“参与暴动”和“管有攻击性武器或管有物品意图损坏财产”等罪名提出指控，并将其案交于香港西九龙裁判法院进行聆讯庭审；后经多次提堂审理，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，其等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人“参与暴动案”终被西九龙裁判法院分别判处<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月至<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年不等刑期，其中，其被以“暴动罪”、“管有攻击性武器罪”等重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；据悉，庭审中其父亲曾多次参与旁听，但后因被确诊为末期肺癌，或可很快离世，遂其辩护律师称其已得终身教训，希望法院能予轻判，然最终遭拒，仍维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。目前疑似在壁屋监狱（香港新界西贡区清水湾道<span lang="EN-US">397</span>号）服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/03/5.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/03/5.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">何喜梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省南阳市<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁的法轮功学员，退休前曾在南阳市沼气（现郑燃南阳燃气）公司任营业所长，一九九七年开始修炼法轮大法，在工作中，何喜梅兢兢业业干好本职工作，多次被单位、建委、省建设厅评为：“先进科室”、“建委十佳职工”、“省建设厅职业道德先进个人”等荣誉。她丈夫帖林峰也修炼法轮大法。一九九九年七月二十日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功，何喜梅和帖林峰曾多次遭中共邪党迫害。何喜梅和丈夫帖林峰，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被南阳市公安局抓捕，关押在南阳市看守所。后获悉，何喜梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，勒索罚金三万元；帖林峰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，勒索罚金一万元。何喜梅刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">何晓丹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省锦州市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日晚，辽宁省锦州市法轮功学员何晓丹、王颖、巩丽娜同时被锦州市古塔公安分局及所辖派出所警察抓捕、抄家。她们最初被关押在锦州凌海隔离，之后被送到锦州市女子看守所关押。大约在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，她们被构陷到锦州市凌海检察院。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月获悉，她们三人都被凌海法院诬判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/25/457131.html#2322423213-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/25/457131.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">何林夏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广西师范大学出版社集团前董事长，此出版社是大陆最先锋和最前卫的出版社，其打造的“理想国”、“魔法象”、“新民说”品牌也在读者和知识分子群体中享有很高的知名度。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，广西检察院官方微信公众平台发布消息：日前，广西壮族自治区人民检察院依法以涉嫌受贿罪对广西师范大学出版社集团原董事长何林夏（正处级）决定逮捕，案件侦查工作正在进行中。据知情人士透露<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月中旬何林夏就被逮捕了，与出版社年初计划出版已故历史学家高华的遗作和独立导演张赞波的作品《大路》被叫停有关，作为董事长的何林夏疑被秋后算帐。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，广西灌阳县人民法院以所谓贪污罪判处何林夏有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10 </span>年，这和其出版一些当局认为比较危险的书有关。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">贺品琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">上海</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">闵行区<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1949</span>年生。</span>家住上海市闵行区马桥镇俞塘村，一九九六年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日在家里被抓捕、所谓“收监”，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月获悉其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。关押机构借口疫情，一直不让家属接见，贺品琴的身体状况令家属十分担忧。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/5/452735.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/5/452735.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">贺瑟琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">女，贵州省黔东南苗族侗族自治州（简称黔东南州）凯里市人，基督徒，贵州省凯里</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">市基督复临安息日教会神职人员，教会聚会点负责人（之一），中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年左右贵州省凯里市基督复临安息日教会聚会点成立以来，因其积极热忱地服务于该教会聚会点中的各项事务，随很快成为教会福音事工活动的中间力量和相关侍奉工作的负责人，并为众信徒及其他侍奉同道所称许；但因其教会聚会点<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多年来一直采取非官方的家庭教会聚会模式，并对中共当局严格把控的“三自教会”管理模式拒不认同和接受，遂遭贵州当局在意识形态上的严苛限制，导致该教会聚会点虽早已向贵州省宗教局提交了请求聚会点合法申请书，但却始终未获审批；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，又因其聚会点信徒不断剧增，聚会点由最先<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个扩建变成<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个，随很快引起贵州省黔东南州当局的极度恐慌，即刻组成立项目组对各聚会点进行全面排查，并将其及教会长老等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名神职人员被黔东南州凯里市警方传唤带走，后被以涉嫌“诈骗罪”刑拘，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人被凯里市检察院以同罪名予以批捕，指控其等因所在教会聚会点“请求聚会点合法申请书”未被国家审批，众信徒所交奉献款均属于诈骗款，故其在教会里的一切敬拜、事工行为等均属违法；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人案在黔东南州凯里市法院统一开庭审理，最终被分别以“诈骗罪”秘判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>—<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年不等刑期；其中，贺瑟琴被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月；另其教会<span lang="EN-US">140</span>万余元奉献款亦被宣判扣押，称将“由凯里市公安局依法发还被害人”；其不服，提起上诉；据称，黔东南州中级法院似乎不愿对其上诉案公开审理，且对辩护律师提交的新证据也无兴趣；二审正在等待中。目前被羁押于黔东南州凯里市看守所（贵州省<span lang="EN-US">/</span>黔东南苗族侗族自治州<span lang="EN-US">/</span>凯里市<span lang="EN-US">/</span>永乐路，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">556099</span>）。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贺云杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贵阳法轮功学员。女、<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年生，贵阳市铁路客运段料库管理员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月中旬，贺云杰和刘淑娅为了帮助市民了解法轮功，发放法轮功资料，期间被人恶告。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，贺云杰和刘淑娅分别被贵阳铁路公安、南明区分局国保、二戈寨派出所警察抓捕、抄家，被关押到五当区三江看守所。被关押了<span lang="EN-US">162</span>天后，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日分别被南宁区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">洪长：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">浙江杭州法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年五十二岁，硕士研究生学历，一人独居杭州。因为遭受多年的迫害，没有固定的生活来源，主要是靠在补习班给小朋友教围棋是来维持生计。洪长在上围棋辅导课的课间时间，教小朋友按照真善忍做好人，遭人恶告，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被杭州市拱墅区公安分局上塘派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月下旬，被杭州西湖区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金五万。洪长上诉到杭州市中级法院。二月底，被杭州市中院裁定维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源： <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://4.31.18.88/mh/articles/2022/3/15/%E6%9D%AD%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E6%B4%AA%E9%95%BF%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4%E5%86%A4%E5%88%91-%E4%B8%80%E5%AE%A1%E4%BA%8C%E5%AE%A1%E5%9D%87%E8%BF%9D%E6%B3%95-440087.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning:
