style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">洪桂连：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">安徽省计生牺牲品和政府不作为乱作为受害人。洪桂连因计划生育国策两次被黄山市屯溪区强制堕胎，此后唯一的儿子又因政府疏于安全生产管理，导致采砂船滥采滥挖河砂，导致家乡河道出现危险溺水而亡，为此洪上访维权，被迫接受政府所谓救助金，却被翻手为云覆手为雨的政府定为敲诈勒索罪。洪桂连出狱后申诉、控告无门，就赴京上访，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，从北京返家后的第二天就被警方以所谓网上逃犯名义抓捕，然后移交给安徽省黄山市警方，现在羁押于黄山市看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">洪海华：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1957</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，湖北省咸宁市通城县沙堆镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月开始修炼法轮功。在中共对法轮功的疯狂迫害中，多次被抓捕、关押，其中两次被劳教，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，洪海华先生被抓捕，后被咸宁市通城县法院庭审；其中<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次开庭，律师做无罪辩护，第<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次申诉仍被枉判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月入湖北省沙洋范家台监狱迫害。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/5/%E6%9B%BE%E4%B8%A4%E6%AC%A1%E8%A2%AB%E5%8A%B3%E6%95%99%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-%E6%B9%96%E5%8C%97%E5%92%B8%E5%AE%81%E5%B8%82%E6%B4%AA%E6%B5%B7%E5%8D%8E%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%83%E5%B9%B4-430457.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/5/%E6%9B%BE%E4%B8%A4%E6%AC%A1%E8%A2%AB%E5%8A%B3%E6%95%99%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-%E6%B9%96%E5%8C%97%E5%92%B8%E5%AE%81%E5%B8%82%E6%B4%AA%E6%B5%B7%E5%8D%8E%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%83%E5%B9%B4-430457.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">候井卫：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京市通州区西集镇法轮功学员。侯井卫是<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被当地派出所抓捕、抄家，不法人员抢劫走大法书、电脑笔记本上台、打印机<span lang="EN-US">4</span>台等本应该受法律保护的私人财物。其家人也被抓捕到派出所，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>天后家人被释放，但派出所派了一些村民监视侯井卫家人。侯井卫被关押在通州区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>侯井卫被通州法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">侯希才：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">在黑龙江省哈尔滨打工的牡丹江法轮功学员。侯希才<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被哈尔滨铁路公安处抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被以“取保候审”的方式放回。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，侯希才又被哈尔滨铁路公安处抓捕，且被批捕。后获悉其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/17/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%83%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-434960p.html#211216215550-2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/17/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%83%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-434960p.html#211216215550-2</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡宝龙：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">内蒙古通辽市蒙古族律师，通辽市蒙嘎立律师事务所负责人。胡宝龙毕业于内蒙古师范大学蒙文系，曾参与八九学运。后从事律师职业，胡宝龙曾代理内蒙古异议人士巴图张嘎案、著名蒙古族维权作家高玉莲案。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2010</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">28</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日，胡宝龙被二连浩特边防警察禁止出境，理由是他涉嫌“危害国家安全”，并被告知其通辽市公安局已经把他列入到不能出境人员名单。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月底开始，内蒙古通辽市、鄂尔多斯市、呼和浩特市等多地的数万学生和家长发起罢课及抗议集会，反对当局加强汉语教学。胡宝龙是一名孩子的父亲，他不久前曾拒绝送孩子上课，并明确反对中共当局推行的“双语教育”活动，因此于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月初被通辽市警方刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡德元：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1944</span>年生，江西省鹰潭市法轮功学员。胡德元为原鹰潭市铁路公安人员，后因坚持修炼法轮功，被开除公职。他曾经多次被劳教、关押，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次被判刑。第<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被枉判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次被枉判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日发放法轮功资料，被警察抓捕、刑拘、构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月获悉他已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源： <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/5/6/2022-5-6.html#zip5"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/5/6/2022-5-6.html#zip5</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">胡吉秀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广州市海珠区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年出生，大专毕业，吉林省德惠市人。她于<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年开始修炼法轮功，十几年来屡遭中共迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，胡吉秀被海珠区昌岗派出所警察抓捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，她被海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，缓刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月四日，她被越秀区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月才从广东省女子监狱回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，胡吉秀在海珠区工业大道沿线和越秀区张贴真相粘贴，遭监控拍摄。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，她被海珠区公安分局警察抓捕，并被抄家。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月九日被海珠区检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被构陷到海珠区检察院。七、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月份，被构陷到海珠区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，胡吉秀被海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，被罚金一万元。她认为判决，向广州市中级法院提起上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，广州市中级法院维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/1/450298.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/1/450298.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">胡今朝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">云南</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">昆明市法轮功学员。胡今朝原是云南省精神病院的主治医生。只因修炼法轮大法，遭到中共残酷残害，<span lang="EN-US">34</span>岁时他被拘留并被剥夺医生的工作；<span lang="EN-US">36</span>岁时他被迫离婚；<span lang="EN-US">36</span>～<span lang="EN-US">39</span>岁时被劳教所迫害了<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">40</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">44</span>～<span lang="EN-US">46</span>岁时被判冤刑关押<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年，他<span lang="EN-US">53</span>岁，再度遭冤刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"> 2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日深夜<span lang="EN-US">11</span>点，胡今朝在家中被昆明市盘龙区公安分局抓捕抄家，他被关押到盘龙区第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月初，当地中共法院对胡今朝判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千元。胡今朝提出上诉，二审法庭维持原判。胡今朝日前已被劫持到云南省第一监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/18/%E5%AE%9D%E8%B4%B5%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8E%E9%81%AD%E8%B9%82%E8%BA%8F-%E5%A5%BD%E5%8C%BB%E7%94%9F%E8%83%A1%E4%BB%8A%E6%9C%9D%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E5%8A%AB%E6%8C%81%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-441418.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/18/%E5%AE%9D%E8%B4%B5%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8E%E9%81%AD%E8%B9%82%E8%BA%8F-%E5%A5%BD%E5%8C%BB%E7%94%9F%E8%83%A1%E4%BB%8A%E6%9C%9D%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E5%8A%AB%E6%8C%81%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-441418.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">胡金慧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，山东法轮功学员，系山东临沂市罗庄区盛庄镇北盛庄村民，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，兰山区公检法在河东看守所内对胡金慧开庭，将胡金慧的电脑、大法书籍、真相资料作为证据。不久，胡金慧被判重刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。约在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，胡金慧被劫持到山东省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/31/447046.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/31/447046.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡天峰：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1981</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，河北省人，深圳市居民，前中国武警部队成员，前缅北雇佣军人，原深圳市某派出所警员，民主维权公民，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。自幼父母离异，跟随母亲在颠沛流离中长大；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年，曾因母亲拔牙发生医疗事故，在家乡求告无门的情况下踏上了茫茫维权之路；维权期间，曾因到北京国家信访局投诉时，在信访局门口竟遭到五六个警卫暴打，随愤而参加了中国武警部队，以期能锻炼出强健的体魄为母亲的不公遭遇讨回公道；在部队期间，曾因听闻缅甸军方在中国边境制造恐怖袭击，炸死无数中国边境人员，而中共当局却为面子和所谓团结，不对此类事件加以重视或回击，其遂聚集了数名热血青年毅然前往边境，希望以此为国效力；但当看到实际情况后，感觉有心无力，随改变认识，毅然加入缅北雇佣军，在热带雨林里与缅军对峙八个月；回国后，<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年，又在深圳市某派出所做警员，期间结识众多仁人志士，并曾对许多陷入生活窘困的民主维权人士慷慨解囊；辞职后，因积极践行民主自由理念，不断为底层百姓不平之事呐喊、为被拐卖儿童奔波、为国家免费教育呼吁，遂遭致中共广东当局的不满与维稳打压；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，胡天峰被广州市警方突然从家中带走，自此失踪；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被广州市国家安全局以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”转为刑拘，至今尚无更多确切讯息。目前被羁押于广州市国家安全局看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日获悉：广州<span lang="EN-US">2020.11.12</span>大抓捕案，胡天峰、范一平、范文成、韦亚妮、赖天明五人被控涉嫌颠覆罪，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月已经秘密开庭，有无律师介入不清楚，是否宣判尚无消息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/1112.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/1112.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">胡勇：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">湖北钟祥市人，基督教华南教会（<span lang="EN-US">SCC</span>）创建人及钟祥交通会骨干成员。曾因其与龚圣亮、徐福明等人共同组建基督教华南家庭教会，是湖北省荆门市钟祥市教会的骨干成员，并积极力促该教会在活动范围和信徒人数等方面迅速发展，随引起中共当局的极度恐慌和强烈不满，在把华南教会定性为“邪教组织”的同时，亦对其及其多名教会骨干成员施以严酷的打击；<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，因与徐福明等人一起被控涉嫌“参与<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月在湖北省钟祥市对受害人谢东报复伤害案”，而被荆门市钟祥市警方以“利用邪教破坏法律实施罪”刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被湖北省荆门市中级法院一审以同罪名判处死刑；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日又经湖北省荆门市中级法院二审，以“故意伤害罪”改判为无期徒刑，剥夺政治权利终身。目前在湖北省某监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡玉兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1946</span>年生，吉林市昌邑区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日发法轮功资料时，被街道人员报给昌邑区司法局，被抓捕、抄家，被关押在吉林市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日胡玉兰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，被关押到长春女子监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡玉莲</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">1944</span>年生，黑龙江省大庆市老年法轮功学员。家住大庆市让胡路区广厦小区，是大庆油田采油六厂职工家属，老伴已过世，她自己独居。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，胡玉莲老人在家中被东湖区公安分局警察抓捕。关押到大庆市杜蒙（泰康）看守。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，让胡路检察院对已<span lang="EN-US">78</span>岁的胡玉莲实施批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，胡路区法院庭审胡玉莲，后于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日下判决书，对老人判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源： </b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/14/443468.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/14/443468.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">胡志琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁大连法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大连公安局国保支队同大连开发区公安分局属下五彩城派出所、湾里派出所、黄海路派出所、海青派出所、董家沟派出所等出动数十个警察，以拦路抓捕、抢劫、入室抢劫的方式在多个地点同时实施多起抓捕法轮功学员案。十名当时被抓捕的法轮功学员被非法批捕：周海燕、胡志琴（女，五十八岁）、来桂芳（女，四十二岁）、时宁瑶（女，三十八岁）、方芳（女，五十四岁）、林景萍（女，四十六岁）、贾秀春（女，四十一岁）、曹娥（女，五十五岁）、武丽艳（女，五十二岁）和刘淑芬（女，七十八岁）。八十一岁的郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被取保候审。后<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月八名法轮功学员被大连开发区法院判刑：周海燕<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，胡志琴<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，来桂芳<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，时宁瑶<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，林景萍<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，方芳<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，贾秀春<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。胡志琴刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黄爱华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东揭阳市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生，广东省揭阳市榕城区梅云镇人，她与丈夫长期在广东东莞做生意。黄爱华利用做生意之便，向顾客讲法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年，黄爱华遭东莞市警察抄家，被抢走大法书籍等财物，并被抓捕到东莞市看守所关押。后得知，黄爱华已经被东莞法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。目前她仍被关押在东莞市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<u><span lang="EN-US">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/20/441229.html</span></u><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄彪：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1952</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，四川西昌市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日下午，黄彪买东西回来，被国安蹲坑抓捕控制后抄家，警察抄走大量私人物品和几万人民币。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日黄彪被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，勒索处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄伯鸣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东省河源市连平县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月出生，大专毕业。在中共对法轮功的疯狂迫害中，他曾两次被劳教，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年被劳教期间，劳教所警察利用吸毒犯对黄伯鸣实施超越人体承受极限的摧残，连续<span lang="EN-US">9</span>天<span lang="EN-US">9</span>夜不准他合眼。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，因讲述法轮功被迫害的真相，黄伯鸣在广东省深圳市被罗湖区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，黄伯鸣被连平县公安局警察抓捕，被关押到连平县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，他被连平县检察院批捕，后来公安警察构陷他的材料被移送到源城区检察院和法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年上半年被河源市源城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>千元。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/8/447419.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/8/447419.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄春玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵根法、黄春玲、刘洪兰、乔华荣四人都是山东省曲阜市的法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，黄春玲在刘洪兰家做客，赵根法、乔华荣夫妻去看她们，刚坐下还没说几句话，曲阜市国保大队人员就进入刘洪兰家，以「非法集会、集体学法」等罪名，将他们抓捕至书院派出所，另外以「把你的包拿过来看一下」为由将赵根法钥匙夺走，在赵根法、乔华荣夫妻二人都不在场、家中无人的情况下抄家，将法轮功书籍、手机、光盘、笔记本计算机、内存卡、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">U</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">盘等几十件物品劫走。第二天，即<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，赵根法被关押在曲阜市拘留所；乔华荣、刘洪兰被送往济宁市看守所进行关押；黄春玲被关押在泗水县拘留所。后赵根法、黄春玲、刘洪兰、乔华荣，被抓捕、关押一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日遭济宁市任城区法院庭审，赵根法被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，黄春玲、刘洪兰被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，乔华荣被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。四人都被非法罚款一万元。黄春玲刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黄红蔚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖北省武汉市法轮功学员<span lang="EN-US">,1961</span>年生，女，家住武汉硚口区长风路城市广场南区<span lang="EN-US">c3</span>栋，武汉远大制药厂退休职工。于<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共迫害法轮功后，黄红蔚遭到骚扰、抓捕、关押、劳教。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日上午十点左右，骆元英、黄红卫在武汉市江岸区三眼桥附近给民众讲真相时遭人恶告，被江汉区国保大队、唐家墩派出所警察抓捕。两人被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。而在<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日拘留结束当日，两人被转为刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，江汉区检察院对骆元英、黄红蔚下达批捕书；<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月上旬将两人构陷到汉阳区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被汉阳法院判刑，骆元英被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、罚款<span lang="EN-US">7</span>千元；黄红蔚被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">4</span>千元。黄红蔚刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/18/447814.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/18/447814.html</span></b></a></span><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄建民：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东揭阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年代生人。家住揭阳市东阳办事处东山村。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日下午，揭阳市榕城区公安分局国保大队伙同揭阳市东阳派出所，到黄建民家进行抓捕抄家。因黄建民在自己家开了商店，经常收到一些真相币，此次抄家抄到了真相币，就成了国保抓捕黄建民的冠冕堂皇的借口了。后黄建民夫妇被关押揭阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，黄建民被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、妻子被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">.</span>刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄金桔：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">她与赵文静、吕月霞、郭春该及张迪<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">为涉</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省商丘巿宁陵县双庙村教会教案成员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日该教会一座兴建中的教堂，遭到数百名政府人员强拆，双方发生争执，教会物品被毁坏，信徒被打伤，数十人包括该<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名负责人被公安带走，后这<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被拘留。他们被指涉嫌“寻衅滋事”及“非法拘禁”罪，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被县检察院正式逮捕。其中张迪是临近一教会的传道人，为协助该教会建教堂，而遭牵连得。目前，所有被捕者被羁押在宁陵县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，该教会成立<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，信徒百多人，当局曾要求加入三自教会不遂。后本案信息全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄俊娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">天津法轮功学员。家住武清区上马台镇王老庄村。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，黄俊娟在善良的向百姓传法时被抓捕，关押在武清看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被武清法院非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并罚金勒索一万元。黄俊娟不服，已上诉。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">黄敏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津滨海新区大港油田的法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月黄敏在厦门被抓捕。被刑事拘留、起诉。黄敏于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被视频开庭，八个月后<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黄琦：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">六四天网人权事务中心创始人、负责人。黄琦<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日晚于家中被带走，其义工蒲飞也失联。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时许被来自棉阳、内江和成都南站派出所的警察<span lang="EN-US">15</span>人闯入家中带走。黄琦<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日生，中国四川人，黄琦毕业于四川大学无线电子系，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年成立了“天网寻人事务所”，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年设立“六四天网”网站。由于网站同时还登载各种批评时政的文章，引发中国当局的关注。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日即六四事件十一周年纪念日的前一天，黄琦被警察捕。在被捕近三年后，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，成都市中级人民法院以煽动颠覆国家政权罪，判处黄琦有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，黄琦刑满获释。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，黄琦改组六四天网为中国天网人权事务中心。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年中国汶川大地震后，黄琦积极参与救灾活动，同时为地震中死亡学生的家长提供帮助，而且在网上撰文揭露“豆腐渣”工程。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日晚，黄琦和天网人权事务中心两名工作人员吃饭时被几名身份不明的人强行塞进一辆汽车带走。后被控「非法持有国家机密」受到刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，黄琦以非法持有国家机密罪名被正式起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日成都市武侯区法院对黄琦案进行了宣判，法院以“非法持有国家机密档罪”，判处黄琦有期徒刑三年。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日黄琦刑满出狱，现定居于成都。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日中共十八大六中全会前夜间与外界失联。后被证实遭随州国保强制传唤。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日上午，著名人权捍卫者、六四天网负责人黄琦被四川省绵阳市法院以“故意泄露国家秘密罪”及“为境外非法提供国家秘密罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，没收个人财产<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。其中“故意泄露国家秘密罪”<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，“为境外非法提供国家秘密罪”<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，数罪并罚执行<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年有期徒刑。狱中身体境况极差，但当局不准保外就医。也不准其<span lang="EN-US">80</span>多岁母亲入狱见面探视。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黄素芹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，辽宁锦州法轮功学员。高中文化，辽宁省锦州市人，曾经在<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被判刑过三年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时许，黄素芹在辽宁省锦州市古塔区早市附近散发真相资料，被抓捕，又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，可能已经被劫持到辽宁女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/12/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%89%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-439959.html#22311213732-8"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/12/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%89%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-439959.html#22311213732-8</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黄晓波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河南信阳市法轮功学员。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">家住信阳市浉河区，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年前开始修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共集团开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，黄晓波向人们讲述法轮功被迫害的真相，被中共邪党抓捕、关押迫害，被迫害流离失所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，流离失所<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年多的黄晓波在信阳市潢川县巍岗乡讲真相时，遭不明真相的人构陷，被潢川县巍岗乡派出所抓捕，被关押在驻马店地区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年上半年，黄晓波被驻马店市驿城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/1/%E6%B2%B3%E5%8D%97%E4%BF%A1%E9%98%B3%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E9%BB%84%E6%99%93%E6%B3%A2%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-440739.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/1/%E6%B2%B3%E5%8D%97%E4%BF%A1%E9%98%B3%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E9%BB%84%E6%99%93%E6%B3%A2%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-440739.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄晓敏：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1962</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日出生，网名“牛鬼的儿子”，河南省新野县籍人，前新疆喀什市疏勒县农三师党校教师，六四民运参与者，自由撰稿人，独立中文笔会会员，四川泛蓝联盟召集人之一。早年曾生长于新疆喀什市农三师伽师总厂，后从喀什农学院农学系毕业，就职于新疆喀什农三师党校任教师；<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年辞职后，前往四川省成都市居住至今，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月成为独立中文笔会会员；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，曾因现场采访鲍俊生等上访人员在四川成都中级法院大门外举行的“链子门”事件抗议示威活动，要求释放<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被捕的“六四天网”负责人黄琦等，并与友人共同拍录像像，发往海内外媒体刊登，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被成都市金牛区警方以涉嫌“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”抓捕、刑拘，同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被正式逮捕，并被关押于乐山市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被乐山市市中区法院一审以同罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，二审依然维持原判，刑至<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被释放；出狱后，因继续参与维权活动，接受外媒采访，在网上发表有关民主维权文章，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-5</span>月，又因积极介入了云南省委党校退休教师子肃发表公开信要求中共<span lang="EN-US">19</span>大开放直选、选举胡德平为总书记事件，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被成都警方秘密绑架，自此失联，家被查抄；其家人为知其下落被迫做寻人启事，后得知其早已被成都警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，其案被成都市金牛区检察院起诉至金牛区法院；至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，被成都市金牛区法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，刑满释放。此前被羁押于成都市看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，又被成都市警方莫名以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，后被转逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日获悉，近期已被成都市金牛区法院以同罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。目前被羁押于成都市看守所。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/4.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/4.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">黄醒民：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省廊坊市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日晚，廊坊市金桥派出所的警察非法闯进黄醒民家，抓捕了他，同时抄走走家里的法轮功书籍等私人物品，包括黄醒民的手机。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，关押持到唐山市冀东监狱第四监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄雪琴：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1988</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，女权独立记者，曾任《新快报》及《南都周刊》的调查记者，关注性别、平权、官员贪污、企业污染、弱势群体等议题，也参与多起<span lang="EN-US">#MeToo</span>案件的报道和为性侵害性骚扰受害人提供帮助和支持。黄雪琴本计划于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年赴香港大学就读法学硕士，但后于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被广州警方以“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，后改指定居所监视居住至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日取保获释。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年，黄成功获得英国志奋领奖学金支持，原计划于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日前往萨塞克斯大学（<span lang="EN-US">University of Sussex</span>）就读发展学硕士。王建兵原计划<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日送别女权记者黄雪琴经香港赴英国留学。但是，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点<span lang="EN-US">,</span>广州警方于王建兵出租屋中<span lang="EN-US">(</span>位于广州海珠区新港西路<span lang="EN-US">)</span>强行将王建兵和即将出国留学的黄雪琴一同抓走<span lang="EN-US">,</span>并查抄了两人的私人财物。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">,</span>王建兵的朋友于黄埔长洲用于储物的出租屋也遭到警方强行撬锁进入搜查<span lang="EN-US">,</span>并带走大量物品和行李箱。据知情人士透露，目前可以确认两人系被广州警方控制，警方均以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”拘留了王建兵和黄雪琴两人<span lang="EN-US">,</span>并疑对双方采取了“指定居所监视居住”措施。主要原因是涉及日常在王建兵他家中的朋友聚会。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，王建兵家属收到广州市公安局发出的“逮捕通知书”，逮捕公函号为特殊的穗公捕通字<span lang="EN-US">[2021]X2</span>。该通知书显示王建兵已于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被广州市公安局以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权”的名义被执行逮捕，黄雪琴家属也拿到了相关通知。黄雪琴与王建兵已于<span lang="EN-US"> 2022 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 3 </span>月<span lang="EN-US"> 27 </span>日正式移送广州市检察院审查起诉。此前黄雪琴曾在未通知家属与律师的情况下，被私下转移至疑似广州第二看守所处单独关押审讯数月，而王建兵也曾被单独关押于其他场所审讯数月。目前二人已重新转至广州第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_1.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_1.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄云敏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄云敏是新疆生产建设兵团农三师图木舒克市的退休法官，因帮助农三师农场职工维权，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被以“煽动民族仇恨、民族歧视罪”拘捕。黄云敏案曾于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日在新疆生产建设兵团喀什农垦法院开庭。后获知黄云敏被转送“法律援助中心”接受所谓的思想教育。并未有判刑信息。后获知，黄云敏因替百姓维权获刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。（<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日黄云敏因会见时告知其妻子自己被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年遭当众殴打。新疆退休法官黄云敏至今家属拿不到判决书。他是因异议学者子肃案被关押的黄晓敏兄长。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黄之锋：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1996</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日出生，英文名<span lang="EN-US">Joshua Wong Chi-fung</span>，基督徒，国籍中国（香港）、英国国民，无党籍民主派人士，荣获美国《时代杂志》<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年度<span lang="EN-US">25</span>名最具影响力少年（之一）之称， “雨伞运动”领军者，香港学运思潮召集人、香港众志秘书长，中国在押政治犯。自幼曾随父母参与教会活动，做义工，热心服务于小区公共事务；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，曾就读香港公开大学，并于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月以优异成绩从大学毕业；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，曾与中学校友林朗彦成立学生组织“学民思潮”，曾多次组织学生游行、集会等，以反对香港政府假借德育及国民教育科向学生进行拥护中国共产党的洗脑教育，从而引起社会各界广泛关注；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，曾受邀出席《城市论坛》，就国民教育议题与其他嘉宾辩论，因表现出色而获公众广泛赞许，并成为全香港反对“洗脑教育”运动全面爆发的导火线；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，曾因参与雨伞运动，主导学生举行“和平占中”罢课集会而被警方拘捕，后被取保释放；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，曾因与林朗彦等人成立香港众志，提倡香港自治，不主张香港独立，同时表明“如无民主自治，只能选择港独”，而成为“不合北京心意的人”；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，曾因重夺公民广场事件而再度被捕，被香港高等法院以“非法集会罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，又被法院以“刑事藐视法庭罪”加获刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月；其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被减刑至<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月；出狱后，因又加入“反送中”运动，表明政府应明确撤回逃犯条例修订草案及撤回<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日百万人大游行定性为暴动的错误，同时指林郑月娥因造成香港人流血而已无资格再当特首，故使港府及中共当局更加不安；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，香港国际机场爆发大规模集结示威在即，因其在脸书上做直播<span lang="EN-US">,</span>呼吁届时游行人数能越百万等，随被警方于<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日在街头带走，并被检方指控涉嫌“煽惑他人参与未经批准的集结”等罪；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因准备前往德国讨论香港情势而又被警方以“违反保释条件” 罪由拘押；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，曾因报名参选区议会选举，而被北京的“硬命令”剥夺参选权；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，曾因中国人大通过《港版国安法》，而被迫宣布辞去香港众志秘书长一职，同时退出香港众志，表明其将在今后以个人身份实践信念；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，因包围香港警察总部案件，其与周庭和林朗彦一同被警方再度关押，期间虽暂获取保，但之后又被收监逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，其三人案在香港西九龙法院被以“煽惑他人参与未经批准集结”、“组织未经批准集结”、“明知而参与未经批准集结”三罪开庭受审，同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被分别裁决，其获刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>个半月，另二人分获<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月和<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月。目前在香港赤柱监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://cppc1989.blogspot.com/2020/12/cppc00953.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">http://cppc1989.blogspot.com/2020/12/cppc00953.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄治萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省南充市高坪区法轮功学员。自从<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共迫害法轮大法以来，黄治萍多次遭到中共的残酷迫害。这之前，曾<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次被劳教、<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次被抓捕到洗脑班迫害、被抄家不少于十次。一家人被抓捕、关押，遭受巨大的身体、精神、经济上的损失。黄治萍的丈夫王道德被迫害含冤离世；孩子生活在恐怖之中；姐姐被迫害成精神病，家中老人含恨离世。黄治萍<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日在龙门菜市场被高坪区公安局国保警察抓捕抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被开庭，随后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">霍晓辉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江哈尔滨香坊区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年年初，哈尔滨疫情严重。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，哈尔滨市香坊区<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员李力壮、霍晓辉、唐竹茵、李艳清、丁燕、焦其华、赵丽华，在车上打电话告诉世人大疫来临莫惊慌，诚念“法轮大法好，真善忍好”。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大庆市让胡路区龙南公安分局在哈尔滨市香坊区抓捕了霍晓辉、李力壮、唐竹茵、丁燕、赵丽华、焦其华、李艳清等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员，以他们拨打“反宣”电话为名，逮捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，大庆市让胡路区法院在侦查事实不清，证据不足等情况下，枉法对哈尔滨李力壮等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员下达判决：霍晓辉被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/3/%E5%93%88%E5%B0%94%E6%BB%A8%E4%B8%83%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B3%E5%8D%81%E5%A4%9A%E5%B9%B4-434311.html"><b lang="EN-US">7</span>年的杨荣丽姊妹。后来一些同工被取保候审，又有一些新的人被抓捕。现在还在看守所的有<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人<span lang="EN-US">: </span>王晓光牧师及妻子杨荣丽，李双平、董勇勇、赵国爱、霍壮平、吴玲娥。这七人于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span minor-fareast;">靳维锋、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">靳玉玲、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">景春、敬慧玲、荆建秋、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">鞠殿红、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">季桂珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1947</span>年生，苏州市法轮功学员，家住苏州市高新区浒关开发区南庄村。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点半左右，苏州工业园区娄葑派出所<span lang="EN-US">1</span>帮便衣，闯到季桂珍家的老旧屋子（苏州皮市街前庙巷<span lang="EN-US">7</span>姬庙弄<span lang="EN-US">5</span>号），实施抓捕、抄家。当晚，季桂珍被“取保候审”放回。之后，季桂珍被构陷到苏州市吴江区检察院、吴江区法院<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，季桂珍女士，被苏州市吴江区法院庭审，近日得知，季桂珍女士被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">季国荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山西</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">太原市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生，家住山西省太原市万柏林区，已退休，于<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮大法。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，季国荣控告迫害元凶江泽民；<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月她被太原市万柏林区龙泉派出所副所长樊昭庆带领数名警察上门抓捕、拘留。季国荣<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日只身前往晋源区金胜村讲法轮功时，被村民诬告，后被金胜村派出所和晋源区公安分局联合抓捕并抄家，随后被刑事拘留，关押到太原市第三看守所，同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被批捕，关押到太原市古交市第四女子看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月辗转得知，季国荣已经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现被关押在山西省晋中市榆次区女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/11/451770.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/11/451770.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">季孝龙：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1976</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，江苏省张家港市人，张家港市杨舍镇名都花苑居民，基督徒，人权捍卫者，民主人士。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾因宣传民主理念而被上海市浦东新区警方以“寻衅滋事”罪由传唤，并被处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾因在网上发文，呼吁民主人士响应“厕所革命”，并在医院、大学等公共场所的厕所门上，用马克笔写宣传语“大病治不起，习胖狂撒币，修宪妄称帝、苦难何时毕！打倒共产党。还政于民，结束民众苦难。推翻习核心，拒走文革路”等字句，短时间内响应者众多，随于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日再次被浦东新区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，又被送到指定居所监视居住；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被以同罪由转正式逮捕，关押在上海市浦东新区看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其案被上海市浦东新区检察院起诉至上海市浦东新区法院；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其最终被该法院以“寻衅滋事罪”一审判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；据悉，羁押期间，警方曾多次以让其“死亡”和用寒冷气温逼迫其认罪，致其身体健康虚弱且生病吐血；其家属曾送羽绒服和《圣经》书籍亦遭拒收；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，刑满获释。此前在上海市白茅岭监狱七监区服刑。因出狱后仍为被封城的上海市民发声，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日再次被上海警方带走，后获悉被刑事拘留。于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被正式逮捕。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2023</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日获悉：季孝龙的案子已经到了检察院。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">羁押在上海浦东新区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">季永成：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东省临沂市法轮功学员，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">家住临沂市蒙阴县桃曲镇（桃墟镇）西陡山村。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，他在临沂市兰山区发放真相小册子，被临沂市公安局兰山分局西郊派出所警察抓捕，拘禁一天一夜后被放回家，由蒙阴县公安局桃曲派出所“监视居住”。此后，临沂市公安局兰山分局西郊派出所警察曾两次去季永成家骚扰，试图抓捕他，都没成功。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，季永城在家中被费县公安局城北派出所及蒙阴县公安局桃墟镇派出所警察抓捕至费县派出所；<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日又被关押到蒙阴县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，季永成被临沂市兰山区检察院批捕，并被关押到临沂市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬获悉，季永成被临沂市兰山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/3/450361.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">纪金睦：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">青岛市胶州市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日在第三人民医院被胶州市中云派出所警察抓捕、关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被黄岛区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万<span lang="EN-US">2</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/5/451529.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span
