8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">姬瑞岭：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北省邯郸市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年已经<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁。家住河北省邯郸市邯山区。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，开元派出所警察闯入明仁医院值班室，抓捕了正在值班的姬瑞岭，并抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被肥乡区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/11/458698.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/11/458698.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">吉白（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川甘孜藏区炉霍县人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，在西藏康区炉霍县境内发生大规模和平示威活动后，中共军警釆取武力镇压，导致云丹为首的多名藏人被开枪打死或打伤，上百人遭捕。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日中共当局对<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名遭捕的藏人进行判决，其中一名藏人被判终身监禁，另有多人遭<span lang="EN-US">1</span>至<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等的有期徒刑。这<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名被判藏人中，已确切得知的有<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名藏人具体情况，其中：吉白，现年<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多岁，被判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">吉力利﹒阿布都拉（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">新疆和田市伊里其乡嘎宗村治保主任<span lang="EN-US">,</span>哈萨克族人权捍卫者。因同村村民买麦提明﹒买吐松经常使用穆斯林方式祷告，被当地公安局指控有“非法宗教活动”之嫌，进而抓捕刑拘，吉力利﹒阿布都拉亦因此被当地公安局指控给“买麦提明﹒买吐松通风报信，让他逃跑”，属于政府认定的所谓“双面人”，所以二人同时被捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，二人同案均被判刑，买麦提明﹒买吐松被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，而吉力利﹒阿布都拉被新疆和田市中级法院重判<span lang="EN-US">17</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2034</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4-5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">贾凤芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">家住北京市平谷区。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，她到平谷区东高村向民众免费赠送真相台历，被东高村派出所警察抓捕。随后，贾凤芝被刑拘，被关押到平谷看守所。。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，贾凤芝被北京市平谷区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，并勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。她上诉后，二审维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日左右，被关押两年之久的贾凤芝被投入天堂河女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/25/%E5%8C%97%E4%BA%AC%E8%BF%91%E5%85%AD%E6%97%AC%E8%B4%BE%E5%87%A4%E8%8A%9D%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-434022.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/25/%E5%8C%97%E4%BA%AC%E8%BF%91%E5%85%AD%E6%97%AC%E8%B4%BE%E5%87%A4%E8%8A%9D%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-434022.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贾国玺：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1965</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，原籍甘肃会宁人，成都电子科技大学毕业以后在广东深圳外贸工作和安家，后以写电脑软件为生。与各地民运人士多有往来，行事低调，很少有人知道他的情况。曾联署过《零八宪章》和多个人权呼吁书。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日贾国玺遭山东省阳谷县公安局刑事拘留，罪名是“颠覆国家政权”。目前被羁押在阳谷县看守所。截至目前，其亲属知晓与否、律师是否已有介入等均情况不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">贾精文：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁锦州市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US"> 1995</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月开始修炼法轮功。在中共对法轮功的迫害中，贾精文曾多次被抓捕、关押。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被锦州市公安局太和区分局入室抓捕，关押在锦州市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，他被构陷到凌海市检察院。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月获悉，其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/3/447186.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/3/447186.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贾乃芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁抚顺市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年生。贾乃芝一九九七年十一月开始修炼法轮功。自一九九九年七月二十日中共江泽民集团开始疯狂迫害法轮功，二十多年来，贾乃芝遭受的残酷迫害数不胜数，多次被抓捕，被羁押在拘留所、自强学校、教养院、看守所、监狱，长时间过着暗无天日的生活，多种酷刑迫害，身心受到严酷的摧残，累计冤狱十多年，自由被剥夺，财产被抢去，受邪恶政策株连，善良的丈夫承受不住压力被迫离婚，年迈的母亲长期思念女儿不得见，含泪而死，孩子得不到妈妈的照顾，遭遇二十多年的迫害，使贾乃芝夫离子散，家破人亡。贾乃芝<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日再次被抓捕，又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被关押到辽宁女子监狱，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月期间检查出肝病大三阳（传染期）。贾乃芝的家属给辽宁女子监狱狱警打了电话，了解一下贾乃芝的身体情况，监狱并没有给贾乃芝医治，家属要求保外就医，监狱狱警说，办不了。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贾榀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">南方街头运动人士、河南籍民主人士。贾榀曾在<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年因言获罪遭广东警方以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，后获释。据悉，贾榀在二十大前去往广西北海市，随后向友人传信说被河南国保带回，从<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日至今再无消息。至今已经超过两个月，目前处于强迫失踪的状态。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/blog-post_77.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/blog-post_77.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贾芹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，河南省人，河南省平顶山市宝丰县闹店镇公民，维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，曾因贾芹丈夫杜海洋跟邻居杜全志因为琐事发生肢体冲突，一周后其丈夫即被警方带走刑拘，后因杜全志被司法部门鉴定为轻伤，故其丈夫杜海洋被河南省宝丰县法院以“故意伤害罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月 ；后又因在其夫的刑事判决书中看到“证人李松献、李清云称杜海洋跟杜全志的肢体冲突发生在<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年”，而<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年其丈夫已被判入狱，故其意识到该刑事判决书明显存在“认定事实不清”，遂开始替夫维权伸冤、讨公道；然而在其替夫维权上访十年余间，不仅未能讨公道，反遭多次被拘捕，并曾三次被判囚，即先是被以“妨害作证罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，而后又两次被以“寻衅滋事罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，因其相继两次进京信访及投诉，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被驻京办截访人员遣回原籍，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其被河南省宝丰县检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”予以正式批捕；据悉，当局此次对其的逮捕决定，意味着其为丈夫杜海洋的“故意伤害罪案”维权伸冤，或将面临第<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次庭审判囚。目前被羁押于宝丰县看守所（河南省平顶山市宝丰县为民路北段，邮政编号：<span lang="EN-US">467400</span>）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/03/blog-post_53.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">贾淑娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">甘肃省白银市会宁县郭城镇法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月出生，家住会宁县郭城驿镇红堡村<span lang="EN-US">1</span>社<span lang="EN-US">95</span>号，农民。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年后，贾淑娟遭到中共当局包括抓捕、关押、劳教、判刑的迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，会宁县公安局国保大队在外面抓捕了贾淑娟夫妇。现得知，她已被当地中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，目前被关押在甘肃省兰州市位于九州岛岛开发区的女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/19/%E4%B9%B0%E5%8D%96%E5%85%AC%E5%B9%B3%E9%81%AD%E5%A6%92%E5%AB%89-%E7%94%98%E8%82%83%E5%86%9C%E5%A6%87%E8%A2%AB%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-441469.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">嘉扬多吉（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治区州阿坝县藏人，是甘孜县色西底乡木西村人，遭捕前以放牧为生。于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14&nbsp;</span>日独自在县城一条街道上开展了和平示威活动，声喊出“允许达赖喇嘛尊者返回西藏”、“西藏要自由”等口号，抗议中共的治藏政策，随即遭到公安拘捕。当局稍后要求嘉扬多吉的亲友们，前往甘孜县公安局登记电话和手机号码，并警告他们不得将此消息传出境外。后信息全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">嘉央洛追（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治区州阿坝县人，阿坝县甲尔多乡孜郎寺僧人嘉央洛追，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年约<span lang="EN-US">35</span>岁。于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日夜晚在马尔康县人民医院门前被当局拘捕。据信僧人嘉央洛追是因为在微信上撰写并发送涉及“敏感”内容的文章，而被中共政府拘捕。后信息全无。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">加尔肯别克·卡生巴依（哈）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新疆维吾尔自治区博尔塔拉蒙古自治州博乐市人，哈萨克族，职业不详，哈萨克国移民，宗教人士，中国在押良心犯。已于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年退休，之前曾多次前往哈萨克国（以下简称哈国）；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，正式移民至哈萨克国；因协助其妻及其两名孩子也移民到哈国，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，从哈国返回中国时，被新疆博乐市当局以“传播宗教极端思想，鼓励新疆哈萨克族人移民哈萨克”为由送入“去极端化培训中心”羁押；后虽有暂短释放，但很快又于同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被博乐市警方收监逮捕；<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，被博尔塔拉蒙古自治州博乐市法院以“煽动民族仇恨，民族分裂罪”、“宗教极端犯罪”秘密判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月</b>；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其逃往国外的儿子珠玛丹<span lang="EN-US">.</span>加尔肯别克因不堪父亲蒙冤入狱被判，被迫向哈萨克国总统、外交部及社会菁英们发出求助呼吁，以期能使其父尽快获救；另据悉，截至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，其家人尚未收到任何官方对其的刑事裁决通知书；其妻、女因此受牵连，妻子图尔逊古丽<span lang="EN-US">.</span>努尔海已于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被原退休单位博乐市达勒特镇中心小学停发退休金，女儿山山古丽<span lang="EN-US">.</span>加尔肯因帮其聘请、委托辩护律师，亦被送入“去极端化培训中心”羁押，至今失联。目前服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">简兰英：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">45</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">岁，家住乐山市中区水口镇谢村。她于<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年因病开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，帅惠兰、简兰英去夹江县农村民宅发送法轮功真相资料，被夹江县国保大队警察抓捕、抄家，被送到乐山看守所关押。帅惠兰、简兰英被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，现被关押于成都龙泉女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/23/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E5%B8%85%E6%83%A0%E5%85%B0%E3%80%81%E7%AE%80%E5%85%B0%E8%8B%B1%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-%E6%9D%B3%E6%97%A0%E9%9F%B3%E4%BF%A1-445293.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/23/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E5%B8%85%E6%83%A0%E5%85%B0%E3%80%81%E7%AE%80%E5%85%B0%E8%8B%B1%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-%E6%9D%B3%E6%97%A0%E9%9F%B3%E4%BF%A1-445293.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">江莲花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">江西省南昌市南昌县莲塘镇法轮功学员，女。江莲花因派发法轮功资料遭人举报，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日在莲塘家中被警察抓捕。后她被关押在莲塘看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月获悉，江莲花被当地法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。据悉，警察欲于年后将她转到江西女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/2022-1-20.html#zip2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/2022-1-20.html#zip2</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江增朝：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，又名江曾潮，黑龙江省绥化市青冈县人，绥化市安达市常居公民，个体小商户，法轮功信仰者，自由信仰权利捍卫者，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始接受并信仰法轮功；<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-9</span>月，曾因时任中共最高领导人江泽民开始打压迫害法轮功，为捍卫自由信仰权利，随进京上访被遣回，并被黑龙江省安达市警方非法关进看守所<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天，惨遭酷刑折磨和毒打，并被戴死刑犯使用的沉重脚镣，后又被青冈县警方继续关押<span lang="EN-US">21</span>天才被释放；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，又被安达市朝阳派出所警方以涉嫌邪教罪刑拘，并送安达市看守所关押<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个多月；<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，曾因坚持锻炼法轮功而被绥化市当局处以劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，且被关在黑龙江省绥化劳教所服劳役；获释后，为生计，且为躲避当局打压和避免家人受牵连，而曾被迫在辽宁省盘锦市靠打工为生；然因其一边打工一边仍不忘进行法轮功宣传，于<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被辽宁省盘锦市警方野蛮拘捕；后其案件被移交到辽宁省盘锦市法院，同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，被该法院一审以“组织利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，并被先送到辽宁省沈阳第二监狱（大北监狱）创二监区服刑，后又转送到大连南关岭监狱（大连市第一监狱）接续服刑；刑满出狱后，其为生计被迫又到黑龙江省大庆市谋生；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，再次因散发、宣传法轮功数据，故而与其妹江洪艳一同被大庆市让胡路区龙南派出所警方以涉嫌“宣传邪教罪”从家中抓走、刑拘，且被分别关押在大庆市林甸县看守所和太康县看守所；后其妹被取保释放，而其仍被继续羁押并被让胡路区检察院以同罪由予以正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，其案在黑龙江省大庆市让胡路区法院开庭审理，终被该法院一审以“组织利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；其不服上诉；后经大庆市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。目前在黑龙江省呼兰监狱（黑龙江省哈尔滨市呼兰区腰堡乡<span lang="EN-US">803</span>信箱，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">150521</span>）服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/03/5.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/03/5.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">姜奎：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贵州省黔东南苗族侗族自治州（简称黔东南州）凯里市人，基督徒，黔东南州凯里市基督复临安息日教会神职人员，教会聚会点骨干成员及带领人（之一），中国在押良心犯。自从参与贵州省凯里市基督复临安息日教会聚会点的敬拜活动以来，因一直致力于热忱服务教会的多种事工活动，随深得教会聚会点长老与众信徒的信任和赞许；但因该教会聚会点<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多年来一直属于家庭教会聚会模式，对中共当局严格把控的“三自教会”管理拒不认同也不接受，虽然早已向贵州省宗教局提交请求教会聚会点合法的申请，但却始终未获审批，故遭贵州当局在意识形态上的严苛限制；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，又因该聚会点信徒不断增多，聚会点迅速由原先的<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个增加到<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个，遂引起贵州省黔东南州当局的注意与恐慌，并迅速成立项目组，对其聚会点进行全面侦查；之后，其及教会长老等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>位神职人员悉数被黔东南州凯里市警方带走，并被以涉嫌“诈骗罪”刑拘，自此失联；后其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人又被黔东南州凯里市检察院以同罪名正式批捕，控其因聚会点申请未被国家审批，众信徒所交奉献款均属于诈骗款，故其一切教会行为属于违法；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人案被黔东南州凯里市法院一审分别以“诈骗罪”枉法判处<span lang="EN-US">12</span>—<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年不等刑期；其中，姜奎被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月；其不服判决，已向黔东南州中级法院提起上诉；二审正在等待中。目前姜奎被羁押于黔东南州凯里市看守所（贵州省<span lang="EN-US">/</span>黔东南苗族侗族自治州<span lang="EN-US">/</span>凯里市<span lang="EN-US">/</span>永乐路，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">556099</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">姜淑梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，沈阳市皇姑区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁。在中共对法轮功持续至今<span lang="EN-US">22</span>年的迫害中，姜淑梅曾被劳教、判刑，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年，姜淑梅被关押在辽宁马三家教养院迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年后，被关押辽宁省女子监狱迫害。累计被关押迫害<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，皇姑区公安分局新乐派出所<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个警察，闯到姜淑梅的家中，抓捕了姜淑梅，并抢走了大法书籍、电脑、打印机等私人物品。姜淑梅被秘密关押到沈阳市看守所。后获悉姜淑梅又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被关进辽宁第二女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/29/%E6%9B%BE%E9%81%AD%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3-%E6%B2%88%E9%98%B3%E5%A7%9C%E6%B7%91%E6%A2%85%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4-434164.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/29/%E6%9B%BE%E9%81%AD%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3-%E6%B2%88%E9%98%B3%E5%A7%9C%E6%B7%91%E6%A2%85%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4-434164.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">姜伟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">辽宁省朝阳市法轮功女学员。姜伟因为坚持真善忍信仰，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被非法劳教三年；<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被非法判刑八年；期间她被迫离婚、遭受酷刑，被关精神病院，被摧残得了胃癌。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，姜伟再次遭绑架，半年后又被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">姜文忠：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">烟台退役军人。烟台海阳市发城镇中夏屋庄村农民。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年因烟台交警违规执法，姜文忠被交警的车撞伤，医生说最低将造成九级伤残。为讨回公道，姜文忠向有关部门控告烟台交警，烟台交警最后同意赔偿<span lang="EN-US">30</span>万，向姜文忠支付了<span lang="EN-US">15</span>万，另<span lang="EN-US">15</span>万转给了发城镇政府。为了讨回这<span lang="EN-US">15</span>万，姜文忠继续控告烟台交警，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底姜文忠到北京后，被海阳截访人员强行带回，从此失去自由。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底被以寻衅滋事罪刑拘，随后被逮捕，初被羁押在海阳看守所，后被转至烟台市看守所。在烟台市看守所羁押至今期间被同室羁押人员殴打过几十次，他曾绝食四天多以示抗争，现虽然已被调换监室，但被殴打的问题依然没有彻底解决，会见时他告诉律师，调换监室后现在开始遭受辱骂，随时可能被打。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/blog-post_17.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/blog-post_17.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">姜志林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新疆博乐市访民姜志林下肢残疾，在博乐市务农。因自治区水利厅新水饮《<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>》<span lang="EN-US">65</span>号文件不落实，造成村民长期用水困难。姜志林为此逐级上访反映，均不但得不到解决，反而多次遭到威胁、殴打、拘留。之前姜志林因为举报村主任贪腐，被警方一再迫害打击，拘留多次，上访拦截抓捕，当地政府一直企图把姜志林构陷入狱。姜志林热心公益，经常以“南国林子”的网名转发微博。他身残志坚，曾在小安妮失学事件中，大力呼吁网民关注，还不断为入狱的郭飞雄等良心犯呼吁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月据知情者透露：姜志林曾签字接受了当地有关基层部门每月一千五百元低保待遇，却被以“敲诈勒索罪”遭当地检察院批捕。姜志林是<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被新疆博乐警方抓捕的，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被当地检察院以“敲诈勒索罪”逮捕。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，新疆博乐姜志林母亲周女士介绍：“正在新疆伊犁新源县哈拉布拉监狱服刑的姜志林，身体虚弱目光呆滞。除了体重明显下降外，目前已经不能正常说话。狱方说是患有脑梗正在接受治疗之中。”姜母想了解更多有关生情况，却被工作人员粗暴拒绝。具体刑期不明。后获悉，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，其案在新疆博乐市法院秘密庭审，终被一审以“敲诈勒索罪”、“诬陷罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年；二审维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月传出其已病危。</b>目前在新疆哈拉布拉监狱（新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州新源县哈拉布拉镇，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">835814</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">蒋凤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北保定市安国市法轮功学员。蒋凤<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被国保大队副队长陈彦青等抓捕、关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被偷偷开庭、判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">蒋益芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">哈尔滨市阿城区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生。蒋益芬一九九五年开始修炼法轮功，身心受益。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日其被国保警察抓捕、关押，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被判刑三年，现在被关押在哈尔滨市女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/24/457088.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/24/457088.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">焦桂春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东省威海市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，女，家住威海市高技术产业开发区。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，她与法轮功学员王策在文登市葛家镇集市讲法轮功时，遭人恶告，被文登市公安局国保大队抓捕，随后取保获释。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，文登市公安局国保警察闯到王策家将王策抓捕走。王策被荣成市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。为躲避迫害，焦桂春被迫离家，在外流离失所漂泊了五个月。她丈夫因经常被警察骚扰、恐吓，精神有些失常。焦桂春在得知丈夫感染新冠病毒后，回家照顾他。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，焦桂春的家人在警察的恐吓、威逼下，把她送到文登市公安局，她被关押到文登看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月获悉：焦桂春被荣成市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/25/459188.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/25/459188.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">焦其华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江哈尔滨香坊区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年年初，哈尔滨疫情严重。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，哈尔滨市香坊区<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员李力壮、霍晓辉、唐竹茵、李艳清、丁燕、焦其华、赵丽华，在车上打电话告诉世人大疫来临莫惊慌，诚念“法轮大法好，真善忍好”。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大庆市让胡路区龙南公安分局在哈尔滨市香坊区抓捕了霍晓辉、李力壮、唐竹茵、丁燕、赵丽华、焦其华、李艳清等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员，以他们拨打“反宣”电话为名，逮捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，大庆市让胡路区法院在侦查事实不清，证据不足等情况下，枉法对哈尔滨李力壮等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员下达判决：焦其华被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/3/%E5%93%88%E5%B0%94%E6%BB%A8%E4%B8%83%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B3%E5%8D%81%E5%A4%9A%E5%B9%B4-434311.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">焦晓华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">哈尔滨的法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生。家住哈尔滨市呼兰区。一九九六年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，焦晓华在向人们传播法轮功时，被哈尔滨市公安局呼兰分局原野派出所警察抓捕，并于第二天关押到木兰看守所。于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，焦晓华被道外区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。后又遭加刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。目前，焦晓华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/13/457686.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/13/457686.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">金汉琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北省郧西县土门镇金汉艳和金汉琴姐妹俩，在<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年从十堰市农校考取了公职单位，后被有关系人的顶替了，姐妹俩还因上访而遭郧西县腐败分子关押到十堰市茅箭区精神病医院<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，导致金汉艳和金汉琴姐妹俩从精神病医院放出来后上访至今无果。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月份，金汉艳和金汉琴姐妹俩再次到北京上访，被郧西县维稳人员抓回关押到十堰市北京小镇五湖商务洒店长期非法拘禁。直到<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，郧西县公安局没收金汉艳和金汉琴姐妹俩的手机后，对姐妹俩以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日郧西县公安局将金汉艳和金汉琴姐妹俩送往十堰市看守所关押看守。金氏姐妹俩失联后，其家属多次找地方派出所询问姐妹俩的下落，郧西县土门镇派出所也告知金氏姐妹俩被刑事拘留的信息，但金汉艳和金汉琴姐妹俩的家属至今未收到办案机关的任何刑事拘留手续。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">金氏姐妹俩虽然信访维权了<span lang="EN-US">25</span>年，但姐妹俩的天性属于温文类型，当局对这种性格的人也以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”关押，再次印证了寻衅滋事罪，已经沦为当局维稳的“口袋罪”。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/blog-post.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/blog-post.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">金汉艳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北省郧西县土门镇金汉艳和金汉琴姐妹俩，在<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年从十堰市农校考取了公职单位，后被有关系人的顶替了，姐妹俩还因上访而遭郧西县腐败分子关押到十堰市茅箭区精神病医院<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，导致金汉艳和金汉琴姐妹俩从精神病医院放出来后上访至今无果。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月份，金汉艳和金汉琴姐妹俩再次到北京上访，被郧西县维稳人员抓回关押到十堰市北京小镇五湖商务洒店长期非法拘禁。直到<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，郧西县公安局没收金汉艳和金汉琴姐妹俩的手机后，对姐妹俩以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日郧西县公安局将金汉艳和金汉琴姐妹俩送往十堰市看守所关押看守。金氏姐妹俩失联后，其家属多次找地方派出所询问姐妹俩的下落，郧西县土门镇派出所也告知金氏姐妹俩被刑事拘留的信息，但金汉艳和金汉琴姐妹俩的家属至今未收到办案机关的任何刑事拘留手续。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">金氏姐妹俩虽然信访维权了<span lang="EN-US">25</span>年，但姐妹俩的天性属于温文类型，当局对这种性格的人也以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”关押，再次印证了寻衅滋事罪，已经沦为当局维稳的“口袋罪”。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/blog-post.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/blog-post.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">金犁：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出生，四川省自贡市人，自由职业者，公民权利追求者，民主异见人士，中国在押政治犯。长期以来，因胸怀公义、倡导民主，主张公民权而活跃于四川省自贡市公民圈；近两年，又因在微信朋友圈中多次转发、宣传有关民主与自由言论，以及参与购买文贵农场股份等活动，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，遂被自贡市高新区警方以涉嫌“资助危害国家安全犯罪活动罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，又被自贡市检察院追加罪名，以涉嫌“资助危害国家安全犯罪活动罪”和“寻衅滋事罪”予以正式批捕；至今其案已被提交到自贡市检察院审查起诉；据悉，受其子金展浩之委托，并以是其朋友的身份名义，包龙军与另一名成都籍律师愿共同为其案代理辩护；但当其二人为了解案件要求会见当事人时，自贡市看守所却以疫情之名拒绝他们会见，同时，自贡市检察院也以涉密为由拒绝代理辩护人复制、拍摄卷宗，仅同意他们做部分摘阅，并有<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余张光盘不让查看。目前金犁被羁押于四川省自贡市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_0.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_0.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">金丽燕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">74</span>岁，福建省宁德市法轮功学员。曾因信法轮功并参与网上法轮功信息资料接受、传送、现金转帐及宣传等活动，而被宁德市国保人员长期跟踪、蹲点监控。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬，金丽燕与肖传雄、陈星光、杨贵媚、杨雄、庄友布、陈开奇、林丽芳、王田等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人先后被宁德市警方抓捕，各人家庭均被查抄。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月其被取保候审，后因其继续从事法轮功宣传活动，又被收监逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被福建省宁德市蕉城区法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>—<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等，其中，金丽燕被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。目前都被关押于福建省宁德市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">金敏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年生，吉林省通化市法轮功学员，原在吉林省通化市通化钢铁公司烧结分厂工作。在中共<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月开始对法轮功的迫害中，她多次遭到抓捕、关押，曾<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次被劳教，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被判刑，累计关押迫害达<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年之久，在吉林省女子劳教所（即黑嘴子女子劳教所）、吉林省女子监狱遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日在吉林市永吉县双河镇被抓捕，被关押在吉林市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月中旬得知，她已被吉林市船营区法院秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，金敏及家属上诉到吉林市中级法院。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月获悉，吉林市中级法院没经开庭，维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。金敏在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日已经被关押到吉林省女子监狱继续关押服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/1/441953.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: </span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/28/451221.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">金晓梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省锦州市凌海市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，锦州市公安局太和分局国保大队共抓捕了十几名法轮功学员，包括：张英玲（<span lang="EN-US">61</span>岁）、金晓梅（<span lang="EN-US">52</span>岁）、康桂云（<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁）、刘玉荣（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、李淑芳（<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁）、陈文学（<span lang="EN-US">77</span>岁），都是老太太。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日获悉，辽宁省锦州市凌海市法院对这名老人下达判决，其中张英玲、金晓梅都被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；康桂云<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；刘玉荣、李淑芳、陈文学皆被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，罚金两千元。金晓梅刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/17/447768.html"><b 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">金永新</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：山东青岛法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年生，现年六十五岁，山东省青岛市四方区人。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，金永新、卞丽训夫妇被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日分别被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年金永新在山东省监狱十一监区遭严管、关禁闭等迫害。金永新被打成脑中风、脑血栓、血压高达<span lang="EN-US">260</span>，被送去医院住院抢救，留下后遗症，手脚不灵活，走路缓慢。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/19/445121.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/19/445121.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">金玉红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江省七台河市法轮功修炼人，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月初因去哈尔滨看望同修家孩子（同修因依兰县国保半夜上家砸门从窗户跳落时绳索断裂至死）时，在校门口被埋伏的依兰县国保抓走，现行政拘留后刑事拘留。期间律师一直未获得会见。当时律师向住所检察室反应情况，检察院住所检察室主人也配合看守所撒谎说人不在看守所了，也不告知人是释放了还是被哪个办案机关转移走了。因为疫情原因，案子<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>号经过检察院两次退补后送到了法院。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月金玉红被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">靳书英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25-27</span>日，刘星、刘玉红、董秀荣、靳书英等法轮功学员被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月获悉：刘玉红被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，刘星<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，董秀荣<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，靳书英<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。靳书英刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/13/458748.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/13/458748.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">靳维锋：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">武汉市武昌区法轮功学员，家住湖北武汉市武昌区。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日上午十点左右，在家中被东亭派出所警察抓捕，被关押到武昌青菱看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月获悉，靳维锋已被当地中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月十六日被关押到湖北省沙洋范家台监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<u><span lang="EN-US">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/12/450633.html<o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%;">靳玉玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">河南省信阳市浉河区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日法轮功学员白玉珍、靳玉玲被信阳市警察入室抓捕，后被构陷至信阳市潢川县检察院、法院，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日在看守所遭开庭。靳玉玲<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁；白玉珍老人<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁，进法庭时，身体走路都不稳。在开庭过程中，靳玉玲、白玉珍一直还被强制戴着手铐。靳玉玲被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">8000</span>元；白玉珍被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。靳玉玲刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/2022-1-20.html</span></u></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">景春：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1954</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，吉林省盘石市人，吉林省盘石市安乐乡村民，维权冤民，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，曾因与同村另一村民发生的一次冲突而被警方于次年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日刑拘，并关押在盘石市公安局东山看守所，遭受严刑拷打；<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，被当地法院利用虚假证据，在未开庭的情况下，以“故意伤害罪”被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，赔偿伤害人医药费<span lang="EN-US">1711.97</span>元；后经其妻刘金艳多次维权上诉，法院才不得不改判其无罪，并于<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日将其释放；获释后，因其就被枉法关押一年一案依法向法院提出国家赔偿申请，遭到法院无理拒绝，遂被迫走上漫长艰辛的维权之路，期间多次遭遇到地方当局的打击与迫害，身心俱损；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年底，因其再次向当地政府提出信访诉求，随被 盘石市警方于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日强行抓捕，并以涉嫌“敲诈勒索（政府）罪”被刑拘，关押于吉林省盘石市看守所；一个月后，又被以同罪名正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，被吉林省盘石市法院宣布重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，经二审裁决，驳回上诉，维持原判。目前在吉林省长春市宽城区兴业监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">敬慧玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四川南充市南部县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年生，家住四川南充市南部县，原南部县农行职工。一九九六年，她开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日上午，在公交车上，敬慧玲给几个学生讲法轮功被迫害的真相，被南部县国保大队副大队长蒙长军等人抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，南部县法院两次对她庭审，均因证据不当而无果。敬慧玲曾质问：到底哪条法律因我发了两个<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘，打了几个电话，就被破坏了法律？即使这样，敬慧玲仍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，后她被转至成都女子监狱继续迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">荆建秋：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郑州市法轮功学员。女，六十多岁，家住河南郑州市上街区。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日下午，周喜云在荆建秋家中做客，她俩一起被荥阳广武派出所警察、荥阳国保大队警察抓捕，被关押在郑州第三看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，在中原区法院南办公区被开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月下旬，荆建秋和周喜云被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，罚款三万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">鞠殿红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，吉林省临江市人，基督徒，云南省临沧市云县基督教一家庭教会传道人，云南教案受害人，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年以来，因其一行多人在云南省多地以家庭教会形式进行基督教传道和发展信徒，势力逐渐壮大，随遭中共云南当局警觉恐慌，很快组成<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>“<span lang="EN-US">YN3</span>﹒<span lang="EN-US">15</span>三班仆人派邪教组织项目”对其主要成员严打迫害；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其及数十人在“云县教案大逮捕”中被临沧市云县警方统一抓捕、刑拘，被关押在临沧市云县临翔区看守所，同时，其住所亦遭查抄，搜走多份传道宣传品、传单、手机以及计算机等对象；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，其及其另外<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人均被以涉嫌“利用邪教组织破坏法律事实罪”转正式逮捕，被控“到云南省多地州市秘密聚会、传经布道和发展信徒，继续鼓吹、宣扬世界末日论，培养组织骨干，为秘密传教布道聚会创造条件和提供便利，重建<span lang="EN-US">'</span>三班仆人派<span lang="EN-US">'</span>组织体系等”，属于违法行为，并将其视为云县教案首犯；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，其被云南省云县法院一审以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律事实罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">15</span>万元；其不服上诉；后经二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日；据悉，其坚称信仰自由、信仰无罪，并称信仰的不是邪教，其所有书籍在官方认可的“三自”教会里都可买到。目前在云南省第一女子监狱（昆明市晋宁县昆阳镇，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">650600</span>）服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/13.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">新疆维吾尔自治区克拉玛依市维吾尔族青年，天津商业大学的在校学生，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年暑假假期回家就再也没有能返回学校。今获悉他已于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被克拉玛依市公安局以涉嫌“煽动民族仇恨罪、民族歧视罪正式逮捕。目前羁押于克拉玛依市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">卡米莱·瓦依提（维）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">新疆阿图什市维吾尔族人，年仅<span lang="EN-US">19</span>岁，目前就读河南省商丘工学院，是大学一年级学生。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，卡米莱在微信上发布了一段有关“白纸运动”的视频。之后不久，卡米莱的父亲接到了警方来电警告，同时她删除了该帖子。但是，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，卡米莱放假回到家乡新疆阿图什市后被警方带走。卡米莱现在已被羁押超过四个月。作为维吾尔女性卡米莱有可能面临遭受酷刑和其他虐待的危险，这令海内外各界高度关注。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/194.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/194.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">卡姆巴尔<span lang="EN-US">.</span>阿穆巴尔大毛拉（维吾尔族）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">新疆和田市哈尼埃里克镇人，维族名<span lang="EN-US">Qamber Amber Damolla</span>，新疆维吾尔族著名宗教学者，在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，在新疆和田市哈尼埃里克镇高中曾有<span lang="EN-US">17</span>名维吾尔族人被中共和田市当局抓捕，指控他们的言行涉及了与国家安全有关的各种罪名，卡姆巴尔<span lang="EN-US">.</span>阿穆巴尔大毛拉亦是其中之一。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日获悉，其终因不与中共新疆当局合作，而被新疆和田市中级法院以“危害国家安全罪”等重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">康桂云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省锦州市凌海市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，锦州市公安局太和分局国保大队共抓捕了十几名法轮功学员，包括：张英玲（<span lang="EN-US">61</span>岁）、金晓梅（<span lang="EN-US">52</span>岁）、康桂云（<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁）、刘玉荣（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、李淑芳（<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁）、陈文学（<span lang="EN-US">77</span>岁），都是老太太。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日获悉，辽宁省锦州市凌海市法院对这名老人下达判决，其中张英玲、金晓梅都被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；康桂云<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；刘玉荣、李淑芳、陈文学皆被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，罚金两千元。康桂云刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/17/447768.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/17/447768.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">康启惠</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：女，安徽省合肥市肥东县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日向民众宣讲法轮功遭抓捕、构陷，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半、罚金八千元。康启惠上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日二审没有开庭，维持冤判，随后康启惠被劫持到安徽女子监狱迫害。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">康卓才丹（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">青海省黄南藏族自治州泽库县多禾茂乡多禾日村人，藏族词曲创作人，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，曾因参与了<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年青海省黄南州藏人学生的“挺藏语”示威游行活动，随被黄南州泽库县警方予以拘捕，直至<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月才被获释；之后其虽被准予获释返家，但因当局恐其再次组织、参与学生抗议活动，遂对其仍进行严密监控，截至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，其身份证件均被没收，欲返回学校亦被禁止，且其在社会上的所有活动都几乎被限；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，又因创作了一首颂扬西藏精神领袖达赖喇嘛的歌曲，并由当地歌手才果广为演唱，之后其两人即遭黄南州泽库县警方抓捕、刑拘；后很快被当地泽库县检察院以涉嫌“煽动分裂国家”等罪予以批捕，并被关押于泽库县看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，其案在青海省黄南州泽库县法院进行庭审，终被一审以“煽动分裂国家罪”、“对外泄露国家机密罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。目前疑似在黄南藏族自治州泽库县监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">克尤木•穆罕默德：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">新疆乌鲁木齐市人，维吾尔族，又被译为克尤木<span lang="EN-US">.</span>买买提，新疆艺术学院副教授，影视演员，主持人，维吾尔表演艺术家，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">早年情况不详，只知其曾因长期在新疆乌鲁木齐市的新疆艺术学院担任副教授，且担任维吾尔青年演员的导师，故而深受维吾尔族裔师生及社会各界人士喜爱、尊敬和推崇；曾被业界及社会大众誉为维吾尔青年表演艺术家和喜剧演员的“表演大师”；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，其突然从舞台、论坛及表演场馆等消失，自此无其任何讯息；后在国际维吾尔人权与民主基金会的不断追踪和查寻下，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日获悉，其被新疆维吾尔自治区乌鲁木齐市警方以不具名罪由已经秘密拘押<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年多；据悉，其在密押期间，一直在被调查中，至今未审不放。目前被羁押地点不明。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/3_27.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/3_27.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">柯有斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西省九江市人，九江市修水县人，民主公民，中国在押政治犯。因喜交友，好时评，常与江西当地多名民主维权公民经常聚集聊天议事，并积极在微信群里发时政性贴文及视频讯息，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，与王林安、李玉荣和陈公安等数名民主维权好友分别被九江地区国保警方传唤带走，次日，其被九江市修水县警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，自此失联；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月中旬，知其又被九江市武宁县检察院以同罪名予以批捕，并与王林安等<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人同属一案；据悉，其等数人此次纷纷被抓，均因中共二十大召开前夕，其等在网络上（主指微信群）讨论敏感话题等，被网警监控知晓，致使当局不安有关；另悉，其在被关押期间，明确表示“宁愿被关，也不悔过”；至今，是否已有律师介入不详。目前被羁押于九江市修水县看守所（江西省九江市修水县宁州镇仁家铺，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">332400</span>）。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_60.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_60.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">肯杰别克﹒阿纳尔别克（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年龄不详，新疆博乐市人，哈萨克族，异见人士。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-3</span>月，因其从哈萨克斯坦国探亲回国后，在微信群里转发了一些移民哈萨克斯坦国的信息，发表了相关言论，并协助本村村民移民哈萨克斯坦国，被当地警方知晓，随于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月底被新疆博乐市警方以</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;;">​​​​</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">“</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出卖国家机密罪”为罪由拘捕，之后一直失联；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月上旬，被新疆维吾尔自治区博乐市法院一审以“泄露国家秘密罪”秘密重判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。目前被关押于新疆博乐市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">肯杰别克•达列力（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">他与</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">纳杂尔﹒叶尔江、哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克、阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克、乌木别提﹒卡斯木、哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗、沙部旦﹒沙伊合、耶尔肯别克﹒达列力、玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗都是新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市巴里巴盖乡人，哈萨克族，穆斯林。其中，肯杰别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁纳杂尔﹒叶尔江<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，乌木别提﹒卡斯木<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁，哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，沙部旦﹒沙伊合约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，耶尔肯别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，，玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，因他们分别在私下里进行了穆斯林传统常规祷告仪式，而被中共新疆伊犁市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰当局知晓后拘捕，遂很快被阿尔泰市地方法院以“非法从事宗教活动”和“从事宗教极端活动”为由分别判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年不等刑期。目前各人具体判刑不详，刑至日期不详，服刑监狱不详，服刑状况及健康程度等不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孔令坡：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东曲阜市后彭村法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日中午，孔令坡在曲阜市董庄镇发放法轮功资料时，被曲阜市董庄派出所抓捕。当天孔令坡被抄家，抄走了家中的大法书籍、视频机、音频机、光盘和和几十元零钱，还抢走了孔令坡的手机，并把孔令坡的妻子抓捕到小雪镇派出所。当天，他妻子被送回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，孔令坡被拘留，被关押在泗水县拘留所，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，没有通知家人，家人曾多次问询无果。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孔文涛，</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男，<span lang="EN-US">66</span>年生，江苏南京人，副主任医师，南京高淳区人民医院消化内科主任，<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年毕业于南京医学院，堪称南京本地的名流望族。因追求民主宪政，期望建立一个法治国家，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初被当局逮捕，今天有消息传来，孔文涛被以颠覆国家政权罪判刑十三年，当庭认罪，且不上诉。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">寇爱梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陕西宝鸡石油机械厂法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日下午，宝鸡市金台公安分局出动了多辆警车、几十个警察，抓捕了宝鸡石油机械厂的八名法轮功学员及家属。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，秦丽杰、李宝莲、寇爱梅三人被关押到宝鸡第二看守所非法逮捕、关押，其他人已于<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被释放回家。后获悉秦丽杰被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，寇爱梅被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半，李宝莲被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。寇爱梅刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邝德英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">云南昆明市法轮功学员。邝德英<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日<span lang="EN-US">13</span>时许，在昆明市西山区海口镇粘土矿出租房内被敲门进来的警察搜查，抢劫了<span lang="EN-US">1</span>些法轮功书籍刊物等，被关押到派出所盘问调查。后被刑事拘留、逮捕<span lang="EN-US">/</span>起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日下午，邝德英被西山法院第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次视频开庭；判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
</div>
